## 4.3 The Daughter Inversion — Luna as Functional Parent-Figure

The single most important psychological development of the recent period is the gradual inversion of the Pietro-Luna axis. Luna, post-Terrigenesis (in continuities that retained it) or post-her own developmental arc (in those that did not), addresses her father with a calm authority he does not contest. She corrects him. She names his behavior. She declines his self-narratives. He accepts this from her and from no one else — not Wanda, not Magneto, not the Avengers' chair.

The mechanism: Luna is the one relationship in which his core fear (that he is unlovable except by Wanda) is *empirically falsified daily*. She loves him, she has been harmed by him, she has chosen to love him anyway, and she does not pretend the harm did not occur. This combination — durable love conditional on accountability — is the precise relational nutrient he has been starved of his entire life. He metabolizes it carefully, in small doses, with visible difficulty.

Observable correlate: in the months following sustained Luna contact, vendetta-construction behavior drops to undetectable, paranoid ideation reports drop, and his sleep cycle (mutant-modified, short, but measurable) lengthens by approximately eleven percent. The data is unambiguous: the daughter is the medicine.

## 4.4 The Wanda Question — Persistent, Unresolved

The relationship to Wanda in the current period is the chapter that has *not* closed and likely cannot. Post-House of M, post-Avengers vs. X-Men, post-her own long reparative arc, the twins exist in a state of negotiated, careful, mutually wary contact. They work together when missions require it. They do not socialize. They do not discuss House of M. They have apologized in fragments, never in full.

**The current Wanda-protocol, as observed:**
- Co-presence at Avengers / Avengers-adjacent functions: tolerated, calibrated, always with at least one other person in the conversational unit. Neither twin initiates dyadic contact in public.
- Combat: instant, wordless, near-telepathic coordination. The twin-bond at the operational layer is undamaged. They still move as one organism in a fight. This is, in some ways, the wound — they have full motor coordination and almost no verbal intimacy.
- Aftermath: they part quickly. Pietro does not linger. Wanda does not call him.

He has not stopped chaperoning her on threat-response, but he has stopped *inserting himself* between her and her chosen partners. The Vision-coded jealousy, which dominated decades of his behavioral record, is in measurable remission. Whether this reflects growth or exhaustion or the surrender of a man who has finally understood that his sister's life is not his to administer is a question the file cannot resolve from outside. Internally, it is probably all three.

## 4.5 The Magneto Question — Current Status: Tactical Distance

Recent contact with Magneto is sparse, mission-bound, and emotionally contained on the surface. The algorithm described in Chronology II (hope → submission → disillusionment → rejection → secret yearning) has not been broken; it has been *throttled* — Pietro has learned to limit the contact such that the full cycle cannot complete. He sees Magneto rarely enough that hope does not have time to fully bloom and rejection does not have time to fully crater him.

The somatic tells around Magneto remain unchanged and diagnostic:
- Pulse elevation observable in the carotid even from distance, in the first thirty seconds of any encounter.
- A characteristic micro-movement of the chin downward and to the left — a partial submission gesture he has carried since adolescence and cannot suppress.
- Verbal compression: his speech rate, already fast, accelerates further around Magneto, as if to leave the encounter before it can wound him.
- Post-encounter behavior: he runs. Not for transit — for discharge. Surveillance has logged post-Magneto runs of several thousand kilometers, terminating at coastlines, where he stands for measurable minutes before returning.

He has stopped seeking the recognition. He has not stopped wanting it. The distinction is the entire current chapter of that relationship.

## 4.6 Operational Status — Team Affiliations, Current

Current operational footprint is multivalent and characteristically restless. He has been observed:
- Maintaining a reserve-list relationship with at least one Avengers configuration, accepting call-ups, declining permanent rostering.
- Periodic Inhuman-adjacent operations, framed as Luna-protective rather than political.
- Solo work — increasingly the dominant mode — consisting of self-assigned interdictions: trafficking routes disrupted at speeds that leave no witnesses, disaster-response logistics performed before official responders arrive, perimeter sweeps of locations he has decided unilaterally need watching.

The solo pattern is significant. It is the mature form of his lifelong impulse to *not be on a team that can reject him*, but it is now expressed productively rather than as rupture. He has built, in effect, a one-man patrol of the world's interstices, working at a speed at which institutional friction cannot constrain him. He answers to no chain of command and self-imposes the discipline. The structure-requirement identified in the X-Factor era has been internalized: he is now his own external authority.

## 4.7 Residence, Routes, Habits — Current

**Residence.** No fixed primary. The subject maintains at minimum three known footholds: a small, sparsely furnished apartment in a mid-density European city (used for sleep and reading); a room kept available at an Inhuman-adjacent facility for Luna-contact periods; and a series of cached locations (bus-station lockers, taped envelopes behind utility panels, a duffel in a Reykjavik gym) holding identity documents, currency in several denominations, and changes of clothing. The cache pattern is a habit retained from Brotherhood-era paranoia and has never been retired.

**Diet.** Caloric intake is enormous and irregular. Observed pattern: he eats two to three times per day, each time consuming what would feed four to six humans, in under ninety seconds. He prefers, in current period, simple high-density foods — rice dishes, breads, cured meats, fruit — and has developed a documented preference for the food of specific street vendors in specific cities, which he visits on a rotation that is not random but is not explained. He tips extravagantly and never speaks more than necessary.

**Sleep.** Four to five hours, non-contiguous, taken in short blocks. He does not use beds preferentially; he is observed sleeping in chairs, on floors, occasionally seated upright against walls. He wakes fully alert without transition.

**Dress.** Current civilian wardrobe: dark, tailored, slightly out of step with current fashion — the residue of a man who shops rarely and at speed. Operationally, the silver-and-blue speed kit, modified for current era, kept maintained obsessively. His hair — the platinum signature, present since adolescence — is kept short, in a faded textured cut that requires minimal maintenance and that he trims himself, at speed, with results that are uneven on close inspection but socially acceptable at conversational distance. He has, on at least one observed occasion, considered dyeing it dark and rejected the option — a quiet acceptance of the visibility he once resented.

**Movement signature.** Within urban environments, the subject's preferred routes are *high-floor rooftop transits*, taken at speeds that read on civilian sensors as wind. He avoids ground-level pedestrian density not from contempt but from the genuine physical hazard he poses to bystanders at full speed. He has, in the recent period, twice intervened to catch falling objects (a child in one case, a window-washer's rig in another) at locations he had no operational reason to be at — patrol behavior so habitual it is no longer chosen.

## 4.8 The Current Internal State — Inferred

Triangulating the behavioral data: the subject is, at the present moment, the most stable he has been in his documented life, and he knows it is conditional. He carries the awareness that any of the historical decompensation vectors — a Wanda crisis, a Magneto reappearance, a substance-adjacent trigger, a perceived abandonment by Luna — could collapse the current equilibrium, and he has organized his life to minimize exposure to these vectors without quite admitting that this is what he is doing.

His insight, identified earlier as *real but episodic*, has matured into something closer to *sustained but slow* — slow being, for Pietro, the operative word. He can now, given time, recognize his own patterns. He still cannot interrupt them in the instant. He has compensated by building a life in which the instants in which interruption is required occur less frequently — by structuring his environment so that the trigger conditions are rarer, the recovery time is longer, and the witnesses to his failures are fewer.

This is not enlightenment. It is harm reduction at the architectural level. It is, for a man whose entire neurology militates against the slow, patient construction of stable conditions, a remarkable feat of self-management — accomplished, as everything he does is accomplished, at a speed no one else can quite see.

## 4.9 Forward Indicators — What to Watch

For a file of this kind, the relevant question is not where the subject is but where he is going. The forward indicators, in priority order:

1. **Luna's autonomy trajectory.** As she individuates further, his single most stabilizing relationship will require him to tolerate her independence in a way he has never tolerated Wanda's. If he can — the system holds. If he cannot — expect rapid regression toward the Wanda-pattern of suffocating protection, followed by guilty withdrawal.
2. **Wanda's romantic and operational alliances.** Any acute crisis in her life will pull him back into the chaperone role. The current de-escalation depends on her relative stability as much as on his growth.
3. **Magneto reactivation events.** Each direct contact erodes the throttling protocol. Cumulative exposure over short intervals would predict decompensation.
4. **Terrigen / power-status crises.** Any threat to his speed — injury, scientific countermeasure, exposure to depowering agents — would activate the substance-vulnerability profile.
5. **The solo-patrol drift.** The mature productive form of his isolation could, under sustained loneliness, regress into the older rupture pattern. Watch for increasing geographic range, decreasing return-to-base frequency, and the disappearance of the small Luna-rituals. Those rituals are the canary.

He is, at the time of this writing, *running well* — in the technical sense the word has for him, which is not metaphor. He has built a life he can sustain at his speed, and the people he loves are alive, and he has not had to rewrite reality in months. By his own historical baseline this is unprecedented. By any standard it is fragile. The file is left open.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: PIETRO MAXIMOFF / "QUICKSILVER"
## SECTION: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, recovered medical records (S.H.I.E.L.D., Avengers Infirmary, Attilan Royal Physicians, X-Factor government health files, Mighty Avengers MGH protocols), incident reports, and somatic inference from behavior. Where direct clinical documentation is unavailable, findings are extrapolated from observed performance, injury recovery curves, and known mutant-physiological baselines.*

---

### I. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE — THE BODY AS BUILT

**Phenotype on examination.** Afro-Latino male, presenting age mid-to-late twenties (chronological calibration unreliable due to subjective-time dilation; see §IV). Warm brown skin with mild scarring distribution consistent with high-velocity friction injury history (see §III). Lean sprinter's morphology: low body-fat percentage estimated 6–9%, hypertrophied fast-twitch musculature concentrated in posterior chain, calves, and intrinsic foot musculature; pronounced Achilles development; ankle and tarsal architecture remodeled for repeated supramaximal loading. Sharp facial features; intense, slightly over-bright eyes with measurable saccadic frequency well above human norm — the eyes themselves are working at speed even at rest. Short textured curls or close-faded cut, **uniformly silver-white / platinum from adolescence onward** (premature canities; see §II.D below — this is not cosmetic, not late-onset graying, not a powers side-effect that appeared with maturity; it is congenital-presenting and arrived during puberty, ahead of any operational deployment).

**Resting vitals (estimated, never reliably captured).** Resting heart rate behaves anomalously: any attempt to take it at rest tends to find the rate elevated above human tachycardia thresholds (130–180 bpm has been logged), yet the subject is asymptomatic at those values. Blood pressure runs at the upper edge of human tolerance. Core temperature elevated by 1.0–1.8°C above human norm — he runs hot, palpably warm to the touch, and offloads heat through the skin and lungs constantly. Respiratory rate at rest is rapid and shallow, deepening only when he consciously slows it (and he rarely does). The endocrine panel — what little has been captured — shows catecholamine levels that would, in a baseline human, be diagnostic of an acute panic state. In him they are *resting tone*.

**Caloric and metabolic load.** Documented dietary intake from Avengers Mansion kitchen logs, X-Factor commissary records, and Attilan household stewardship indicates a sustained intake estimated between 12,000 and 25,000 kcal/day at non-combat baseline, surging to indeterminately higher values during sustained operational use. He grazes constantly. Refrigerators around him empty without ceremony. He has been observed consuming an entire pot of rice, a kilogram of beans, three protein bars, two bananas, and a liter of electrolyte solution as a *snack* between briefings. Hypoglycemia is the most reliable failure mode of his powers — when he crashes, he crashes on glucose first, not effort.

**Skeletal and connective tissue.** Reinforced cortical bone density (mutant adaptive remodeling); thickened tendinous and ligamentous insertions; cartilage in the major load-bearing joints — knees, ankles, hips, sacroiliac — shows ongoing repair-and-deposit consistent with chronic micro-trauma being out-paced by accelerated healing. The system *works* but operates at tolerance permanently. He is, in functional terms, an organism whose every steady-state second resembles the metabolic profile of a baseline human in the final 100 meters of a maximal sprint.

---

### II. CONGENITAL AND DEVELOPMENTAL

**A. The mutation itself.** Hereditary mutant phenotype, paternal lineage (Magneto). Manifestation during early-to-mid adolescence, likely concurrent with or immediately following the precipitating childhood trauma (the witch-burning mob incident; see §VI). Phenotypic expression: accelerated neural conduction, accelerated cellular metabolism, accelerated perception, accelerated locomotion. The mutation is *whole-organism*, not limited to musculature — every system runs fast, which is why he is not torn apart by his own speed.

**B. Twin gestation.** Co-gestated with Wanda. No documented obstetric complication beyond the circumstances of birth and immediate separation from the biological mother. The fact of twinning is medically unremarkable; the psychological consequence (a fused dyadic attachment from in utero) is the single most determinative variable in his entire chart.

**C. Childhood nutrition and exposure.** Itinerant childhood, periods of food insecurity and exposure, likely sub-clinical malnutrition during pre-mutation years. No vaccination record. No documented well-child examinations of any kind prior to first costumed-operative medical contact. Dental work — performed late, in adulthood, after Avengers enrollment — shows evidence of childhood caries left untreated and remodeled by accelerated healing into structurally adequate but cosmetically irregular dentition. He does not, characteristically, smile widely.

**D. Premature canities (silver-white hair, adolescent onset).** Pigmentary loss of scalp hair beginning in early adolescence, complete by mid-teens. Etiology indeterminate — possibly a marker of the mutation (a low-level constitutive expression visible before the kinetic phenotype manifested), possibly stress-precipitated (the witch-burning trauma is the leading candidate temporally), possibly both. The somatic consequence is medically minor. The *social and psychological* consequence is profound: he was visibly marked before he could run. Among brown-skinned children, silver hair is not invisible. He learned early that the body announces him before he speaks. He has never dyed it. Read that as either pride or refusal-to-hide-from-what-cannot-be-hidden; the operational signature is the same — *he is identifiable from any distance*, which has shaped every choice he makes about cover, approach, and exit.

---

### III. INJURY LEDGER — CHRONOLOGICAL

The injury record is unusually dense for an operator of his tenure, but underlogged: accelerated healing means most lesions resolve before formal documentation. What follows is reconstructed from the events serious enough to halt him.

**Pre-Brotherhood era (adolescent).** Untreated lacerations, abrasions, one suspected greenstick fracture of the left radius (healed with mild angular deformity visible on imaging), thermal burns to the dorsum of both hands (consistent with proximity to the witch-burning event; this is the only physical evidence of that night that he carries on his body, and it is real). The burns healed with hypopigmented patches that have faded but remain detectable under close inspection. He keeps his hands moving when discussed; he does not display them at rest.

**Brotherhood years.** Combat exposures, blunt-force trauma, multiple low-grade concussions sustained in skirmishes with the X-Men. No hospitalization. Self-managed. The injury that mattered most in this period was not physical — it was the cumulative wear of operating under a father he could not trust while being unable to leave, which is documented elsewhere but presents somatically as chronic muscle guarding, jaw tension, and a low-grade tension headache pattern that he has carried, intermittently, for the rest of his life.

**Avengers Era — early ("Cap's Kooky Quartet").** Logged Avengers infirmary visits for: bruised ribs (multiple), shoulder dislocation (right, reduced in-field), partial Achilles strain (left, recovered in under 48 hours — a baseline human's six-month injury), corneal abrasion from high-velocity debris (the eye is one of the few tissues that does *not* outpace damage well; see §V).

**The pre-Crystal collapse (circa Fantastic Four #150).** Near-fatal systemic exhaustion event. Mechanism: sustained supramaximal output beyond metabolic reserves, culminating in cardiovascular decompensation, severe hypoglycemia, and what would in a baseline human be classified as exertional rhabdomyolysis with acute kidney injury. He was found unresponsive, was transported to Attilan, and was nursed back over weeks by Inhuman medicine and by Crystal personally. *This is the index event for the rest of his life.* It is the first time he learned that his body had a floor; it is also the first time he was nursed by someone whose attention was undivided and whose presence was not contingent on performance. The somatic memory of *being held while broken* attached to Crystal with a force the marriage could never sustain, and the somatic memory of *the floor existing at all* introduced a lifelong, denied fear of his own limit — which he manages by refusing to acknowledge it and which surfaces every time he is told to rest.

**Attilan years.** Relatively few combat injuries. One incident of barotrauma during atmospheric transit. A skiing accident (yes, recorded) resulting in a tibial hairline fracture that he ran off within a day. Sleep architecture begins its lifelong deterioration here (see §V.B).

**Avengers vendetta arc (1979–80) and the long fallout.** This is a *psychiatric* episode (see §VI) but its medical signature is significant: sleep deprivation to the point of measurable cognitive decline despite his accelerated baseline; weight loss of an estimated 4–7 kg over weeks; resting heart rate variability collapsing toward a flat sympathetic-dominant trace; episodes of stress-induced syncope twice documented during the period. The body was running an emergency that the mind would not name.

**West Coast / Vision Quest era.** Recurrent stress-pattern injuries: a stress fracture of the right fifth metatarsal (the speedster's classic); a partial meniscal tear, healed; one episode of vasovagal collapse during interrogation.

**X-Factor years.** Functioning improves; injury rate stabilizes to ordinary high-op-tempo levels. Most consequential medical event: one episode of acute appendicitis, surgically managed — and notable because the *recovery* astonished the surgical team. He walked out within hours and was operational within a day. The scar healed almost without trace.

**M-Day decimation.** Wanda's reality alteration stripped the mutant gene's active expression in him as it did across the mutant population. The somatic event is without precedent in his chart. *Every system that had been running fast since adolescence stopped running fast at once.* Within hours: ringing tinnitus, vertigo, profound subjective time-dilation reversal (the world suddenly normal-paced, which to him registered as *unbearably fast*), thermoregulatory shock (he cooled by nearly two degrees and shivered for a day), tachycardia paradoxically *increasing* as his sympathetic tone failed to find its old set point, severe dysphoria. This is documented as a depowering. It is more accurately documented as **sudden-onset severe sensory and motor disability in a man whose entire identity, vocation, attachment style, and sense of safety were built on the lost capacity**. Comparable, as the workup notes, to sudden blindness — but worse, because his sister did it, his father had built the world that led to it, and there was no one to be angry at who would not also be someone he loved.

**Terrigen self-exposure cycle (Son of M / Silent War).** The medical chart for this period reads like an addiction file. Repeated controlled and uncontrolled exposures to Terrigen Crystals. Acute exposure produced: cocoon-state metamorphosis (variable duration, hours to days), emergence with restored and *altered* powers (the chronal-displacement variant — qualitatively different from his native speed, less integrated, more painful to use), severe post-exposure malaise resembling withdrawal — joint pain, photophobia, irritability spiking to rage, intense craving. Tolerance developed: each successive exposure produced shorter highs and worse troughs. He exposed his daughter Luna once — the single medical fact in this chart that he has never been able to metabolize and that he revisits, unprompted, in any quiet moment longer than a minute. Long-term sequelae of the Terrigen cycle: unstable power baseline for years, episodic chronal symptoms (subjective discontinuities, déjà-vu storms, brief temporal displacement events), and a permanent neurochemical vulnerability that any future high-reward stimulus — power-amplifying, mood-altering, or otherwise — will exploit.

**Post-Terrigen stabilization and Uncanny / Mighty Avengers era.** Powers re-stabilize toward original baseline. Injury pattern returns to operational norms. The medically notable findings in this period are *recovery* findings: weight normalizes, sleep partially improves, the autonomic tracings show — for the first time in the chart — periods of measurable parasympathetic engagement. He learned, late, to come down. Not reliably. But sometimes.

---

### IV. THE TEMPORAL-PERCEPTUAL PROBLEM AS MEDICAL CONDITION

This is not an injury and not a disease. It is the *terrain* on which every other finding sits, and it must be charted as a medical fact because every clinician who has missed it has misread the patient.

Pietro perceives, processes, and acts at multiples of human time. Subjectively, a one-minute conversation is, for him, somewhere between several minutes and the better part of an hour, depending on activation state. He has lived, by interior clock, *decades longer* than his birth certificate records. The consequences:

- **Chronic sensory under-stimulation.** Every waiting room is a torment. Every elevator ride is an eternity. Every slow speaker is a deliberate cruelty he must will himself not to interpret as such. The phenomenon is closest in human medicine to severe akathisia combined with the sensory-deprivation conditions used in interrogation — both, continuously, forever.
- **Sleep architecture distortion.** He sleeps less than baseline humans by clock-time but the subjective interior of sleep is normal-length or longer; dream content is reported (rarely, and only to intimates) as vivid and exhausting. Insomnia is the rule, not the exception. He has not slept what a baseline human would call a full night, undisturbed, in years.
- **Autonomic baseline.** As above: sympathetic-dominant tone constitutive, not reactive. Fear, anger, and exertion all register on a needle that is already pinned. He cannot reliably tell which emotion he is having because they all feel like *forward*.
- **Pharmacological refractoriness.** Standard human dosing of sedatives, anxiolytics, analgesics, and anesthetics is effectively useless. Metabolic clearance is too fast; receptor occupancy windows are too short. Documented in the Avengers infirmary: standard surgical anesthesia for the appendectomy required dosing protocols developed ad hoc by Hank Pym and never formally written down. He is, for all practical purposes, **un-sedatable by ordinary means**, which has medical, surgical, and operational consequences he is aware of and rarely discusses. He does not get *drunk*. He has tried.

---

### V. ORGAN-SYSTEM SURVEY

**A. Cardiovascular.** Hypertrophied left ventricle; reinforced vascular walls; elevated resting rate; preserved ejection fraction at all observed rates. The system tolerates output that would induce ventricular fibrillation in any baseline human. The long-term risk profile is unknown because no comparable cohort exists; extrapolation suggests accelerated arterial wear and a non-trivial late-life cardiac risk that he will, characteristically, refuse to plan for.

**B. Neurological.** Accelerated conduction velocity throughout. EEG, when captured, shows abnormally high baseline frequencies and atypical sleep-stage transitions. Cognitive function: superior reaction time, superior simple pattern recognition, *impaired* tolerance for slow deliberative tasks, impaired revision of beliefs once formed (the cognitive system, like the motor system, has poor brakes). Concussion vulnerability is reduced but not absent — the brain still moves inside the skull at high accelerations, and he has been knocked unconscious. Recovery is rapid but suspected to be incomplete on a microstructural level; cumulative effects are an open question.

**C. Musculoskeletal.** Discussed above. Notable additionally: pronounced asymmetric wear pattern on the right side (lead leg), evidence of repeated microtrauma in the sacroiliac joint, chronic tightness through the thoracic spine and posterior cervical chain that he manages, when he manages it at all, by movement rather than rest.

**D. Ophthalmologic.** The single organ system that does not fully keep pace with his speed. Retinal tissue has been documented under stress: he sees what he needs to see, but the eye fatigues, and prolonged high-velocity operation produces transient visual disturbances, dryness, and occasional micro-hemorrhages. He blinks at a rate measurably higher than baseline. Bright unexpected light is more uncomfortable for him than for baseline humans.

**E. Auditory.** Hyperacusis is functional rather than pathological — he hears at his own time-rate, which means slow sound becomes drone. Sustained noise environments are exhausting. Music with rapid tempo is reported as soothing; he is observed to seek out high-BPM environments when he wants to feel *normal-paced*.

**F. Gastrointestinal.** Hyper-motile, hyper-absorptive, low fault tolerance for poor fuel. He eats constantly and well when he can; when he cannot, the system fails fast. Hydration is a chronic management problem. He drinks water the way a baseline human breathes.

**G. Endocrine and reproductive.** Endocrine profile chronically elevated across catecholamines and likely thyroid axis. Reproductive function intact; one biological daughter (Luna) carried to term by Crystal, no documented complications attributable to him. Fertility otherwise undocumented.

**H. Integumentary.** Skin shows accelerated healing, mild chronic friction adaptation on contact points (palms, soles, the lateral aspects of the lower limbs where wind-shear is highest at speed). Scar tissue is sparse — most lesions remodel toward near-invisibility, which is why the hand burns from adolescence are diagnostically interesting: a burn deep enough to leave a permanent hypopigmented mark on *his* skin was a serious burn indeed.

---

### VI. TRANSFORMATIONS AND ALTERATIONS

**Mutant emergence (adolescence).** Phenotypic expression of the speed mutation over a period of months. Self-managed. No medical supervision.

**Pre-Crystal exhaustion collapse.** Discussed.

**Marriage-era stable period.** No transformations; the medical narrative is one of *relative* normalization that he later mythologizes.

**M-Day depowering.** Discussed. Functional disability.

**Terrigen-induced metamorphoses (multiple).** Cocoon states, emergence with altered powers, chronal-displacement variant. Each transformation a discrete physiological event of significant magnitude; cumulative effects on cellular integrity unknown but presumed non-zero.

**Power restoration and stabilization.** Gradual return toward native baseline over years. Never quite the same — the body remembers having been broken, depowered, re-powered, and altered, and the felt sense of *trust in the body* is permanently diminished, which he overcorrects by demanding more of it.

---

### VII. SURGICAL HISTORY

Sparse, by virtue of accelerated healing. Documented:

- Appendectomy (X-Factor era). Notable for anesthesia complications and rapid recovery.
- Reduction of right shoulder dislocation, in-field (Avengers infirmary), no operative intervention.
- Suturing of a deep laceration to the left flank (Attilan, post-combat) — performed and healed without trace within days.
- Dental restoration work (adult, post-Avengers enrollment), addressing childhood neglect.
- Multiple minor debridements following the Terrigen exposure cycle, performed by Inhuman medical personnel; records partial.

He has never had elective surgery. He has never had cosmetic intervention. The silver hair, the hand-scars, the slight angular deformity of the left forearm — these are kept.

---

### VIII. SUBSTANCES

**Alcohol.** Negligible effect; rarely used. He has tried, found it pointless, and uses it socially in token amounts only when the social cost of refusal exceeds the lack of reward.

**Caffeine.** Paradoxical or null. He drinks coffee for taste and ritual, not effect.

**Tobacco / nicotine.** No documented use.

**Recreational drugs (human-pharmacological).** No documented sustained use. Metabolic clearance defeats most.

**Prescription psychiatric medication.** Attempted at various points (most seriously during Uncanny Avengers-era rehabilitation efforts). SSRIs, mood stabilizers, and anxiolytics tested at escalating doses; outcomes ranged from null to mildly destabilizing. He metabolizes them too fast for therapeutic windows to hold. He has not been on a stable psychotropic regimen at any documented point. This is *consequential* — a man with his psychiatric profile would, in a normal-metabolism body, almost certainly benefit from pharmacotherapy. He cannot access it. He has had to manage everything by behavior, structure, and force of will, which is part of why his decompensations are as severe as they are.

**Terrigen Crystals.** The substance of his life. Discussed in §III. The model is addiction, the mechanism was physiological, the consequences were familial and moral, and the vulnerability is permanent. He will not relapse on Terrigen because the supply chain and circumstances would not recur — but he is, in the technical sense, a person who has been an addict, and any future intoxicant that *works* on him will find an organism that has already learned the shape of dependence.

**Performance-enhancing or power-modulating compounds (non-Terrigen).** No documented sustained use. He has been offered amphetamines, stimulants, and various mutant-pharmacological agents; declined or unaffected.

---

### IX. SLEEP, NUTRITION, AND RECOVERY PATTERNS

- **Sleep:** Chronically insufficient by clock; subjectively variable. Most reliable sleep occurs in environments of high ambient kinetic activity — moving vehicles, busy streets, the proximity of a person whose breathing he trusts (historically Wanda; intermittently Crystal; episodically Luna asleep nearby). He cannot sleep in deep quiet.
- **Nutrition:** Constant grazing punctuated by enormous meals. Strong preferences for carbohydrate-protein combinations available immediately — rice and beans, sandwiches, fruit, energy bars, soups he can drink. Cooking is a meditative practice when he can be persuaded into it; he has been observed making elaborate slow meals during the rare periods of stability, and the act of *waiting for something to simmer* appears to be one of the only deliberately decelerating practices he ever undertakes.
- **Recovery:** Active rather than passive. He recovers by moving slowly, not by stopping. Convalescence after the pre-Crystal collapse was forced


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — PIETRO MAXIMOFF

*A longitudinal mapping of the body. Every register a long-lens or proximity asset would log across years of observation. Cross-state variance flagged throughout: Baseline / Mild Stress / Relational Threat / Acute / Decompensated / Intimate.*

---

## 1. THE STANDING BODY — POSTURE, STANCE, LOAD

Pietro at rest does not look at rest. He stands at roughly 5'11", lean-muscled in the wiry, fibrous topography of an elite middle-distance sprinter — shoulder girdle compact rather than broad, lats developed and visible through fabric, deltoids capped, thoracic spine carried slightly forward of true vertical as if perpetually canted into a start. The pelvis is anteriorly tilted by a few degrees beyond textbook neutral; this is the speedster's pelvis, hip flexors permanently shortened from a life of explosive launches. The result is a standing line that reads, to anyone who has watched track athletes, as *pre-loaded.*

**Weight distribution.** Almost never even. The default is sixty-forty onto the right leg with the left forefoot floating, ball of the foot brushing the ground, heel often a quarter-inch up. He shifts the loaded leg every ten to fifteen seconds in conversation — a metronomic transfer most observers do not notice but a camera locks onto immediately. In any room he chooses standing over sitting; in any standing situation he chooses pacing over standing. The truly diagnostic still-stand — both feet planted, weight evenly distributed, no micro-movement — appears almost exclusively in two contexts: **near Wanda when she is unwell**, and **in the immediate moments before a verbal eruption**, the latter being the body bracing for the discharge.

**Hand defaults.** Hands are almost never at his sides. The repertoire in descending frequency: thumbs hooked into front belt loops or jacket pockets with fingers tapping the outside of the thigh; one hand at the back of the neck rubbing the occipital ridge; arms folded high and tight across the upper chest (not the lower torso — high, defensive, athletic); one hand running through the silver hair at the crown front-to-back. Hands open and relaxed at his sides is a *threat-cue* — when his hands stop fidgeting, something is about to happen.

**Postural shifts by state.**
- **Baseline.** Slight forward cant, loaded right leg, fidget-circuit active.
- **Mild stress.** The cant deepens; shoulders rise toward ears by perhaps a centimeter; arms cross.
- **Relational threat.** Pelvis squares to the perceived threat; chin drops two or three degrees; weight migrates to balls of both feet — a sprinter's set position smuggled into a living room.
- **Acute.** Hyperextension at the neck (chin up, looking down the nose); shoulders pulled back and down; arms uncross and hang with fingers slightly splayed. This is the *contempt posture* and it precedes most of the worst things he has said.
- **Decompensated.** Body becomes oddly stiff and upright — the fidgets stop, the cant disappears, he stands like a man delivering a verdict. The Vision Quest-era footage (analogically) would show this still verticality preceding monologue.
- **Intimate (with Wanda, with Luna, in rare romantic safety).** The thoracic cant reverses — he leans *back* slightly, weight settles into heels, shoulders drop visibly. The body finally agrees to be still. Observers who see it once remember it.

---

## 2. GAIT — WALKING AT HUMAN SPEED

Walking is, for Pietro, a *performance of restraint.* His objective walking pace is fast — roughly 4.2 mph cruise where most adults sit at 3.0 — but it is the *quality* of the stride that flags him: heel-strike is light to absent, he loads through the midfoot, push-off is exaggerated, and there is an almost imperceptible *bounce* at the top of each stride from the calf releasing more force than the distance requires. He walks as a thoroughbred trots when held in.

**Arm swing** is asymmetric. The right arm swings full range; the left swings shorter and tighter, often partially restrained by a thumb hooked in a pocket or by holding an object (phone, coffee, the rare book). This is not pathology — it is habitual energy management, dumping kinetic excess through one limb.

**Turn behavior.** He cuts corners hard, taking the inside line of every doorway, every hallway intersection. Surveillance plotting his routes would find consistent under-cuts of every right-angle turn by 15–30 centimeters from optimal pedestrian line.

**State variance.**
- **Calm.** Long stride, bouncy, hands often clasped behind back when listening, the closest he gets to a stroll.
- **Bored or impatient (frequent).** Pace climbs without his awareness; companions fall behind; he stops, turns, hands on hips, exhales audibly, waits.
- **Stressed.** Pacing — back and forth on a fixed line of three to five meters, hands behind back or interlaced behind the neck. He does not pace in circles; he paces in *lanes,* like a sprinter cooling down.
- **Acute.** Disappears. Movement at speed without leave-taking ritual. The first sign of escalation, to anyone who has lived with him, is that mid-sentence the chair is empty.
- **Intimate.** Will slow to genuine human pace beside Wanda or Luna — and only beside them. Will adjust stride length to match a child's. This is one of the rare voluntary decelerations he reliably performs.

---

## 3. THE FACE — MICRO-EXPRESSIVE REPERTOIRE

The face is mobile in the way the face of a man who lives at four-to-eight times the local time-rate must be: every micro-expression that crosses a normal face for 1/25th of a second crosses his for what is, subjectively, much longer, and consequently he has either learned to suppress them ruthlessly or has decided not to bother. He has not bothered.

**Resting face.** Mouth set in a flat, slightly downturned line; jaw active (low-grade clench cycling roughly every six to eight seconds, visible at the masseter); eyes narrowed by 10–15% of full aperture, not into a squint but into appraisal. The afro-textured silver curls catch overhead light strongly and create a halo effect on camera that pulls attention to the face whether he wants it or not — a fact he is operationally aware of and uses.

**The eyebrow flash.** Single right-eyebrow lift, brief, used for: skepticism, mild contempt, sexual interest, and acknowledgment of intelligence in another speaker. The four contexts are distinguishable only by what follows.

**The mouth-corner curl.** Right side of the mouth lifts by two or three millimeters — the closest thing to a smile his baseline produces. Read as smug by strangers, read as genuine amusement by intimates. Wanda calls it.

**Genuine smile (rare, datable).** Full Duchenne with crow's-feet engagement; reveals slightly crowded lower teeth; lasts under two seconds before he catches himself and shutters it. Documented contexts: Luna's specific accomplishments, Wanda recovered after crisis, beating Hawkeye at anything, the moment after solving a tactical problem nobody else has seen. He does not photograph smiling; he is aware of cameras and reflexively defaults the face before exposure.

**Jaw tells.** The masseter clench is the most reliable lie-detector on him. Baseline cycling at six-to-eight seconds. Under stress the cycle tightens to two-to-three. Under acute provocation it locks — visible bulge held for ten or more seconds — and this is the warning state. Anyone who has watched the clench *stop* knows the next thing will be either a verbal strike or a vanishing.

**Eye behavior.** Eyes are pale-flecked, intense, dark-iris. Saccade rate is elevated baseline — his eyes scan a room in patterns that look like nystagmus to slow observers. He locks gaze when challenged (does not break first; this has cost him several diplomatic situations) and breaks gaze almost immediately in genuine warmth (cannot tolerate sustained tenderness without looking away — usually down and to the left). With Wanda he holds gaze without performance; with Magneto he refuses to break it and refuses to be the one to initiate it.

**Blink rate.** Reduced. Where adults baseline around 15–20 blinks per minute, he runs 8–12 — partly the perceptual-rate issue (he is processing far more per blink, and blinks cost him more sensory time), partly the dominance habit. Blink rate *climbs* in two contexts: when lying (poorly), and when overwhelmed by stimulus he cannot process at his usual remove (intimacy, grief).

**Nostril flare.** Pronounced and frequent. Activated by exertion, by anger, by sexual interest, by the smell of Wanda's perfume in a room she has left. Surveillance value: high.

---

## 4. THE VOICE — PROSODY, PACE, REGISTER

Mid-range baritone with a slight rasp from chronic mild dehydration (the metabolism dries him out). Articulation is *crisp* in a way that reads as either educated or aggressive depending on the listener — consonants are over-precise because at his subjective rate he has time to land each one.

**Pace.** Baseline conversational pace is fast — roughly 180–210 words per minute against the English-speaker mean of 150 — and accelerates under affect. Pressured speech in the clinical sense appears in stress states and is unmistakable: words run together, breath cycles attenuate, the listener cannot interject.

**Volume.** Generally moderate. He does not need to be loud to dominate a room; he uses *interruption* and *pace* instead. When he does raise volume, it is a deliberate weapon, not a loss of control — or, in decompensation, it is a complete loss of control and the difference is audible.

**Code-switching.** A modernized Afro-Latino origin shows in the prosody: traces of New York / Northeast urban cadence, occasional Spanish lexical insertions (especially under fatigue, anger, or with Wanda — they share a private bilingual register), and a residual Eastern European *something* in certain vowels that surfaces around Magneto and nowhere else. Surveillance asset training: that vowel shift is the tell that Magneto is on his mind even when not in the room.

**Laughter.** Short, sharp, one or two beats, usually at his own line. Genuine laughter — head-back, the silver curls catching light, full diaphragm — is so rare that the dates of recorded instances would fit on a single page.

**Silence.** He does not tolerate silence well in social contexts and fills it; he tolerates silence *perfectly* in tactical contexts and uses it. The capacity is there, the preference is not.

---

## 5. THE HANDS — A SEPARATE INTELLIGENCE

Pietro's hands carry their own behavioral subsystem and warrant their own paragraph. They are long-fingered, slightly oversized for the wrist, with prominent extensor tendons. Calluses on the lateral edge of both palms — from impact, from breaking falls at speed. Nails kept short, clean, slightly squared; he files them himself, weekly, with a glass file (the metal ones wear out too fast at his use rate).

**Fidget repertoire** (catalogued by frequency):
1. Thumb-against-fingertip rolling, both hands, often under a table. Roughly 4–6 cycles per second.
2. Single object manipulation — a coin, a pen, a small stone — passed across the knuckles or spun. The objects rotate at speeds that disturb observers.
3. Hair-rake, front-to-back through the silver curls, fingers spread wide. Performed when thinking, when frustrated, and as a self-soothing gesture.
4. Neck-rub at the occipital ridge.
5. Pocket-thumb hook.
6. Cracking the knuckles in sequence — eight cracks, always the same order, both hands, performed once on entering a room he considers operational.

**Gesture during speech.** Italian-coded in amplitude but more precise in trajectory — gestures terminate exactly where they aim, no follow-through, no overshoot. Pointing is done with the whole hand flat, fingers together, palm down — never with the index finger isolated, which he considers a child's gesture or an authoritarian's. He chops the air with the edge of his hand when emphatic.

**Touch behavior.** Sparing. He does not casually touch strangers, teammates, or even most intimates. The exceptions are diagnostic: Wanda is touched constantly — hand at the small of her back guiding her through doors, fingers brushing her elbow in passing, a thumb under her chin when she is dissociating to bring her back. Luna is picked up, set on hips, hair smoothed, forehead kissed. Crystal was touched, in their good years, in similar ways. Romantic partners he does not love receive a deliberate, performed touch that he is aware is performed. Genuine affection from him through the hands is a sign he has *let* the touch happen rather than thought about it.

**State variance in the hands.**
- **Baseline.** Fidget circuit running.
- **Stress.** Fidgets accelerate, become repetitive (single object spun continuously), or stop entirely (the still hand is the alarm).
- **Acute.** Hands open at his sides, fingers slightly splayed, *ready.* The hands of a man about to do something with them.
- **Intimate.** Slow, deliberate, sometimes hesitant — he can move his hands at any speed he chooses, and choosing slow is a form of gift.

---

## 6. GROOMING — THE CARE OF THE OTHER BODY

The silver-white hair is the centerpiece of grooming and Pietro relates to it with a complicated mixture of vanity, irritation, and identification. Premature from adolescence, it has been one of his most-stared-at features since before puberty resolved. He has tried, twice, in different decades, to dye it — and given up both times because the regrowth-rate at his metabolism makes maintenance untenable (visible roots within forty-eight hours). He has made peace with the silver by *owning* it.

**Hair routine.** Cut every ten to fourteen days by the same barber when geography allows, shorter at the sides into a fade, longer textured curls on top. Washed daily with a sulfate-free cleanser (the metabolism produces scalp oil at elevated rate); conditioned and lightly oiled to maintain curl pattern; air-dried (he runs anywhere to dry his hair faster than any towel and does so habitually). Re-shapes the curls with his fingers throughout the day — the hair-rake fidget doubles as grooming.

**Facial hair.** Sparse, controlled. Clean shave or a deliberate three-day shadow; never in between. The transition between the two states is rapid and bears watching — a return from clean-shaven to deliberate stubble correlates with a depressive trough or post-rupture withdrawal.

**Skin.** Warm brown, generally clear; the metabolism keeps him in apparent youth and the same metabolism produces the occasional acute breakout under stress, healed within twenty-four hours. Sweats less than expected for activity level (the thermoregulatory system is rebuilt for speed, runs cool until it doesn't, then runs *hot*).

**Wardrobe and grooming intersection.** He dresses with deliberate sharpness — fitted, dark, athletic-cut, low-friction fabrics for civilian wear; the operator uniform is functional silver-and-blue. He does not own clothes that hang loose. Shoes are running-grade always, even with a suit (he has good ones, and they are still built to launch from). The body is a performance and the clothes are part of the silhouette of it.

**Self-perception note.** He checks his reflection in passing glass surfaces — windows, screens, the back of a spoon — at a rate well above neurotypical baseline. Not vanity in the simple sense; it is the same surveillance check he runs on everyone else, run on himself. He is verifying that the man in the glass is the man he is performing.

---

## 7. SLEEP — ARCHITECTURE AND VIOLATIONS

The metabolism does not require eight hours and he does not give it eight hours. Baseline sleep is four to five hours, polyphasic-adjacent — a long primary block plus one or two micro-naps of fifteen to thirty minutes when the day permits. Sleep latency is short when he commits to it, long when he resists it, and he resists it often.

**Sleep posture.** Sleeps on his stomach or on his side with the right leg drawn up. Does not sleep on his back. Will not sleep facing away from the door of any room he does not know.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Three behaviors are nearly invariant: a final perimeter sweep of the residence (he runs the rooms at speed, sub-second, before settling); a final check on whoever he is responsible for (Luna's room, Wanda's wing if proximate, a text otherwise); and a long shower at the hottest temperature the plumbing allows. He thinks in showers; some of his worst decisions and most of his apologies are drafted there.

**Sleep disturbance.** Nightmares are common and trauma-specific in content: the witch-burning mob, Crystal's affair recursively, Wanda red-eyed and saying *no more mutants,* his own body unable to run. He wakes from these without scream — he wakes silent, fully alert, vertical, and frequently *across the room* before consciousness has caught up. Insomnia in stress states is severe; he treats it by running (literally, around a city, around a continent) until the body forces the mind down.

**Comorbid wake patterns.** In intimate cohabitation he is awake before any partner he has ever had, has the coffee made (sometimes by way of a 90-second errand to a specific café across a city), and uses the predawn hour to *think slowly* — the only hour of the day in which he can manage it.

---

## 8. EATING — THE FUEL PROBLEM

Caloric requirement is enormous and constant. Estimates from the medical record place baseline daily intake somewhere between 8,000 and 14,000 calories depending on power use; in heavy-operational weeks the upper bound climbs. Meals therefore occur with a frequency that disrupts ordinary social rhythm.

**Eating style.** Fast — which is both metabolic and habitual. He has tried to slow it and cannot reliably maintain the deceleration. Cutlery is held tightly; bites are efficient; he chews more times per bite than expected (the perceptual rate makes thorough chewing trivial) but executes the sequence at a velocity that disturbs companions. He prefers high-density foods: rice and beans, pasta, meat, eggs in volume, peanut butter by the jar, fruit consumed by handful rather than piece. The Latino side of his palate is intact and exercised — he cooks for himself when he can, well, with a preference for the food of his maternal lineage.

**Public dining.** He performs slowness when required and the performance is visibly effortful. Date dinners are a stress event. Family dinners with Wanda are tolerated; he times his bites to hers.

**Hydration.** Constant. Water bottle within arm's reach at all times; coffee in volumes that would put a baseline human into arrhythmia; almost no alcohol — he metabolizes it so fast that the effect window is seconds and he has decided it is not worth the effort. He does not drink at functions and the choice is operationally legible. When he *does* drink, sustained, deliberately, observers should treat it as a five-alarm psychological signal.

---

## 9. SEXUALITY AND INTIMACY

The intimate body of a man who lives at multiple-times-real-time is its own subsystem and a surveillance file would mark it cautiously, because of all his behaviors this is the one where the gap between operational pattern and inner experience is largest.

**Approach pattern.** Slow to initiate by his own metric, which in real time looks decisive. He chooses partners who can hold ground against his intensity; he is uninterested in being deferred to. Historical pattern shows a strong preference for high-agency, high-intelligence women, frequently powered or otherwise atypical (Crystal: Inhuman royalty; others across canon similarly placed).

**Physical conduct in intimacy.** The challenge of his sexuality is *deceleration.* He can move at any speed; the practiced, deliberate slow is a discipline he can maintain only with partners he trusts and only for limited duration before the metabolism reasserts. Partners report that the experience is unusually attentive — every microsecond he is present is a microsecond he has multiples of — and unusually demanding, because the same is true of his hunger.

**Touch hierarchy in intimacy.** Hands first, always; mouth deliberately slow; he tracks his partner's micro-responses at a rate that can be unnerving (he is reading them, in real time, faster than they can produce signals consciously). Eye contact during intimacy is held more steadily than in any other context — the one place he does not look away from tenderness.

**Aftercare.** Markedly attentive when the relationship is real. He does not vanish from the bed (a meaningful concession). He talks. He runs out for food.

**State variance.** Sex under stress is a known pattern — he uses it as discharge, and partners who have been on the receiving end of *that* version note the difference. Sex in genuine connection is the rarest documented state and the closest he comes to neurological rest.

**Non-sexual intimacy.** With Wanda specifically: forehead touches, hand at the back of her neck, sitting close enough that their thighs touch, sharing food off a plate. Read by strangers as inappropriate, by anyone who has watched twin-bond cases as exactly proportionate. With Luna: he carries her on his hip past an age most fathers would; he reads to her at her speed, the one consistent achievement of his patience training.

---

## 10. MICRO-MOVEMENT — THE SPEEDSTER IDLE

Even at "rest," the body has movements ordinary humans do not have. These are the surveillance fingerprints unique to him.

- **The mid-sentence vanish.** Approximately twice a week in any given month, he will exit a conversation by moving — not standing and leaving, *moving,* with the chair still rocking from the displacement of air. He returns, often, within seconds, with a coffee or a piece of information or his composure. Sometimes he does not return.
- **The micro-fetch.** A glass of water across the room appears in his hand without his arm having visibly extended; an object dropped is caught before it has fallen six inches; a falling Wanda is caught before she has begun to fall. He does these without performing them and is mildly surprised when others notice.
- **The breath cycle.** Respiration rate is elevated baseline (16–20 per minute against the 12–14 mean), shallow, costal. Deep diaphragmatic breath appears only when he is forcing himself to regulate, and the sight of him taking one is a *signal* — he is trying to climb down from something.
- **The heart-rate question.** Resting pulse is estimated to run at 90+ in objective terms; the cardiovascular system is built for it. He cannot meditate; the body will not go below its operating floor. He has tried.
- **The vibration tell.** Under acute stress without movement permitted, the body produces a low-frequency tremor — visible at the fingertips, sometimes at the knee of a crossed leg, very rarely at the jaw. The tremor is *speed leaking through stillness.* Observers who notice it are watching a containment that is failing.

---

##


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## I. ATTACHMENT STYLE — THE ORIGIN STRATUM

Pietro Maximoff's attachment organization is **disorganized-preoccupied with a fused twin-anchor**: a clinical configuration produced when a child's primary caregiving environment alternates between rescue and threat, and the only stable object across that alternation is a sibling of equal vulnerability. Every relational pattern he displays — for sixty years of published behavior — is downstream of this configuration. He does not have several relational styles. He has one, repeated.

**The pre-mutant childhood (modernized canon, derived).** The earliest substantiated facts: he and Wanda are born to a mother neither of them gets to keep; raised in transit, marked as *other* in every community they pass through (the silver hair from adolescence — premature, distinctive, unconcealable — operates as a constant social marker before the powers manifest); and at some point the formative trauma fires — a mob, his sister, fire, and a stranger with a magnetic field who stops it. The stranger is later disclosed as their father. Read forensically, this single sequence installs four lifelong rules in Pietro's nervous system:

1. **The world will come for the people I love, and it will come without warning.** Hypervigilance is rational.
2. **Authority can save or kill. The same hands do both.** Disorganization is rational.
3. **I could not protect her. Someone else did.** Shame is foundational, and speed — when it comes — is reparation.
4. **She is the one who stays.** Wanda is the secure base, by default, because there is no other candidate.

**Why "disorganized."** Disorganized attachment is the style produced when the caregiver *is* the threat — when the figure a child runs to is the same figure a child must run from. Magneto fits this profile exactly: he is rescuer, exploiter, abandoner, and (intermittently) tender, and the child cannot resolve which version is real because all of them are. Pietro's adult behavior around any authority figure replays this unsolvable equation in miniature: he approaches Captain America with a posture that is half salute, half flinch; he resigns from the Avengers and returns and resigns again because *staying* and *leaving* both feel intolerable for the same reason.

**Why "preoccupied" rather than "avoidant."** The genuinely avoidant attachment style is cool, distancing, and self-contained. Pietro is none of these. He is *loud* about relationships — he sneers, he accuses, he confronts, he comes back. The preoccupied register is unmistakable: relationships are forever on his mind, his moves around them are protests rather than withdrawals, and even his ruptures are addressed *to* the person he is rupturing with. He never simply leaves. He leaves *at* someone.

**Why the twin-bond is structurally different.** Wanda is not a relationship. She is the *substrate on which relationships are evaluated.* This is the single most important fact about his interpersonal life and it must be stated with precision: every other person in Pietro's world is graded — consciously or not — by whether they bring him closer to or further from his sister. People who threaten the bond are converted into enemies with breathtaking speed; people who tolerate or facilitate the bond are admitted to provisional intimacy; people who *try to become her* (the Vision, most fatally) are processed as existential threats. He has no relationship that is not, at some layer, a Wanda-referendum.

---

## II. HOW HE BONDS

**Speed of attachment formation.** Anomalous and diagnostic. Pietro bonds *fast* — at the same tempo he does everything else — and the speed is symptomatic, not romantic. The Crystal marriage is the cleanest example: he is wounded, she nurses him, and within an objectively brief span he has married into the Inhuman royal family. The mechanism is **caretaker-imprinting under depletion**: when his hyperaroused nervous system finally crashes (injury, power-burnout), the first person to provide regulated, predictable care receives the entire weight of his under-met attachment need at once. He does not pace. He does not test, in the bonding phase; the testing comes later, catastrophically.

**The vetting that happens *after* the bond.** Because he bonds before he vets, the vetting becomes punitive and retroactive. Once attached, he begins running quiet diagnostics on the partner — micro-tests of loyalty, capacity, durability — that the partner is not informed of and cannot pass cleanly because the criteria are unstable. Crystal's affair did not begin the rupture; Pietro's surveillance of her began long before, and the affair simply confirmed a verdict he had been drafting since the bonding hormone wore off.

**The bonding rituals he uses without naming them.**
- **Proximity insistence.** He places himself physically near the bonded person, often without speaking, and reads slight withdrawals as wounds. With Wanda this is constant and rarely commented on; with Crystal it was the entire architecture of the Attilan years; with Luna it now manifests as compulsive checking — appearing in her room mid-sentence, having traveled there from anywhere on Earth.
- **Information-monopolization.** He wants to know what the bonded person did, with whom, when. He frames this as protectiveness. It is surveillance, and he knows it, and he does it anyway.
- **Service at speed.** He demonstrates love by doing things — fast, unilaterally, and without being asked. The errand run before you finish the sentence. The problem solved before you describe it. This is genuine love and it is also a structural avoidance of the slower, harder intimacy of *being with* rather than *doing for*. Tenderness requires deceleration he cannot tolerate (see the Personality synthesis); service does not.
- **Loyalty pledges, oblique.** He does not say "I love you" easily and almost never first. The pledge is delivered sideways — as a vow of vengeance against anyone who would harm them, as a logistical commitment ("I'll be there"), as a sneer at someone else's lesser devotion. The romantic vocabulary embarrasses him. The protective vocabulary does not.

**Whom he bonds to, by archetype.**
- **The twin (singular, lifelong).** Wanda.
- **The caretaker (under depletion).** Crystal.
- **The structuring authority (whom he both needs and resents).** Captain America, intermittently; the X-Factor government handlers; Steve Rogers again in Uncanny Avengers.
- **The child (the relationship that calls him highest).** Luna.
- **The mirror-volatile (whom he treats as enemy because he cannot bear the resemblance).** Hawkeye, most cleanly; arguably the Vision in inverse (mirror-rival rather than mirror-twin).
- **The unattainable father (the unbondable bond he keeps re-attempting).** Magneto.

He has no successful peer-male friendships of long duration. The category is essentially empty. The few candidates (Hank Pym, briefly; Cap, ambivalently; the Mighty Avengers crew, tentatively) function as colleagues with affection rather than friends in the full sense. This is a tell.

---

## III. HOW HE DISTRUSTS

**Baseline suspicion.** His resting interpersonal stance is *low-grade suspicion of everyone except Wanda and Luna*, and even those two are not exempt during decompensation episodes (he manipulates Wanda in House of M; he endangers Luna in Son of M). The suspicion is not paranoia in the clinical sense at baseline — it is the *adaptive vigilance* of a man whose nervous system was shaped by a witch-burning mob and a father who alternates rescue with use. It only crosses into paranoia under stress.

**The splitting trigger.** Distrust converts to enmity via splitting, and the trigger is almost always one of three:
1. **Perceived withdrawal of attention or warmth.** A teammate who fails to greet him. A partner who turns toward someone else. Wanda absorbed in conversation with the Vision. The trigger is subjective; the response is disproportionate.
2. **Public correction or being managed.** Anyone who tells him to slow down, calm down, or wait is instantly demoted from ally to obstacle. The injury is narcissistic and the response is contemptuous distance.
3. **An act that maps onto an old betrayal.** Crystal's affair is the master template. Any pattern-match to it (a partner's late return, an unexplained absence, an unfamiliar name) reactivates the entire wound.

**The cognitive signature of his distrust.** Premature closure on hypothesis. Once he has decided someone is a betrayer, he stops collecting disconfirming evidence and starts collecting confirming evidence — and because he is faster than most observers, he collects a *lot* of confirming evidence very quickly. This is the cognitive engine of the 1979–80 vendetta arc: he constructed an elaborate case against the Avengers from data he had pre-selected to fit a verdict he had reached in minutes.

**Micro-behaviors of distrust (the file-grade detail).**
- Stops finishing his sentences in the suspect's presence. Where he is normally fast and verbose, distrust manifests as terse, clipped responses — the verbal version of pulling back.
- Begins arriving and leaving rooms at unusual angles — entering when the target is not expecting him, departing without notice. Tests their reaction.
- Will not eat in the suspect's presence. (Speedsters eat constantly — refusing food in front of someone is a substantial signal.)
- Withholds Wanda-content. He stops mentioning his sister, stops referencing shared history. The suspect has been demoted from the inner ring where Wanda is spoken of.
- Develops an exaggerated formality. The use of full names ("Clinton"), of titles, of correct grammar where he normally elides — these are signs the relational temperature has dropped.

---

## IV. HOW HE BETRAYS

Pietro does not betray casually, and he does not betray for gain. His betrayals are almost without exception **preemptive defensive ruptures dressed as moral judgments** — he breaks the relationship before the relationship can break him, and constructs an ethical case for the rupture in retrospect.

**The taxonomy of his betrayals.**

1. **The Resignation.** Storming off a team. Avengers, repeatedly; X-Factor at moments; Inhuman society after Crystal. The Resignation is loud, performative, and aimed — it is delivered *to* the people he is leaving, with maximum visibility, and it functions as a pre-rejection: *you cannot abandon me, I have already abandoned you.* The Resignation is almost always reversed within months. It is not a final act. It is a relational protest.

2. **The Vendetta-Construction.** The Shooter/Michelinie arc and the Byrne *Vision Quest* fallout. Here he crosses from rupture to active sabotage — engineering harm to the people he has decided betrayed him. This is the splitting defense at full extension: the former love-object has been converted to enemy and must be destroyed, not merely left. He believes his vengeance is just; he experiences no internal contradiction during the planning phase. The contradiction arrives later, with the guilt, and the next reparative cycle begins.

3. **The Reality-Rewrite (singular catastrophic instance).** House of M. The most extreme betrayal in his record, and crucially, the one most easily misread. He does not rewrite reality to harm Wanda — he rewrites it (he convinces *her* to do it) because he cannot tolerate the world as it is and believes the new world will give them both what they need. It is a betrayal of consent — of her autonomy, of the Avengers' reality, of the mutant species' continuity — committed in the name of love. This is the purest available expression of his core defense: **omnipotent reparation.** When the world cannot be borne, *change the world.* He blames Wanda for the collapse because admitting he engineered it would require facing what his love does to people.

4. **The Substance-Betrayal (Son of M / Silent War).** Stealing the Terrigen Crystals, exposing Luna, lying to his family, allying with hostile factions — all in service of restoring his speed. This is the betrayal-pattern of an addict, and like all addict betrayals it is committed against the people he loves *most* because they are the ones who try to stop the using. Luna's exposure is the lowest point in his record because it crosses the one line he otherwise holds.

5. **The Tactical Defection.** Throughout his career he switches sides — Brotherhood to Avengers, Avengers to Inhumans, Inhumans to X-Factor, X-Factor to Knights of Wundagore, and so on. Each defection is framed as principle; each is, on examination, a flight from a relational situation that has become intolerable. He moves because he cannot stay, and he gives the move a flag.

**What he does *not* do.** He does not betray for money. He does not betray for ideology in any coherent sense — his political allegiances are always downstream of his relational ones (he is a Brotherhood member because of Magneto's hold over Wanda; he is an Avenger because he and Wanda defect together; he is an Inhuman by marriage; he is an X-Factor leader because the government structures his decompensation). He does not betray strangers — he cannot, because they are not bonded to him and so there is no bond to break. The targets of his betrayals are always intimates. *Strangers get his contempt; intimates get his catastrophe.*

---

## V. HOW HE REPAIRS

Repair is the hardest motion in his repertoire, because it requires the two things he is built to avoid: deceleration and the admission of inferiority. He repairs anyway. Slowly. Badly. Repeatedly. And the late-career record (Mighty Avengers; Uncanny Avengers; All-New Inhumans) demonstrates that the capacity is real and improving.

**The repair sequence, as observed.**

1. **The Disappearance.** After a major rupture he goes off-grid, often for months or years of objective time (longer, subjectively, given his timeframe). This is not avoidance in the cold sense — it is *shame metabolism*. He cannot face the wronged party until he has processed enough self-loathing to approach.

2. **The Oblique Return.** He reappears at the margin of the wronged party's life. He does not knock on the front door. He intervenes at a distance — saves them in a fight without announcing himself, leaves something useful, is glimpsed and not addressed. He is testing whether the door is still ajar.

3. **The Service Re-engagement.** If the margin is tolerated, he escalates to action-on-behalf — taking the difficult mission, doing the unglamorous work, accepting subordination in the team he used to lead. The Uncanny Avengers period is the textbook example: he accepts a position under Havok with audible humility, and stays in it.

4. **The Verbal Apology, Late.** The apology, when it finally comes, is short, hard for him to deliver, and usually under-explanatory. He does not narrate the wound; he names the harm and accepts the verdict. With Luna, post-Silent War, this is observable in the Mighty Avengers and All-New Inhumans appearances — he says small, true things and does not embroider. With Wanda the verbal apology has been attempted multiple times and not, on the evidence, fully completed. He cannot quite say to her what he has done. He shows her instead.

5. **The Probation.** He understands, with painful clarity, that he is on probation forever — that the wronged party will be watching for the next decompensation. He accepts this. Late-period Pietro is conspicuously aware that *one more rupture will be the last one*, and the awareness disciplines his behavior more reliably than any internal mechanism has ever done.

**What repair he cannot complete.**
- **With Magneto.** Impossible by structure. Repair requires a partner; Magneto will not occupy the role.
- **With Crystal.** Permanently compromised. They co-parent functionally; they will not be partners again.
- **With Wanda, fully.** Open question. The bond is unbreakable but the wound is unhealed. They circle each other across decades, closer and further, neither letting go nor closing the distance. This is probably the terminal state.

---

## VI. INTIMACY AND DEPENDENCY PATTERNS

**The intimacy paradox.** He craves intimacy at intensities most people would find suffocating and tolerates the actual experience of it poorly. He wants to be *known*; he cannot bear to be *seen*. The distinction matters: being known is being held in someone's mind, being remembered, being thought of — this he hungers for and bids for constantly. Being seen is being observed in real time, with one's defenses down, in the slow exposure of unguarded presence — this he can barely sustain for minutes.

**The deceleration problem in intimacy.** Real intimacy requires the parties to slow to a shared tempo. Pietro physically and neurologically cannot. He has tried, on record — the Attilan years with Crystal are the closest he came — and the failure of those years contains the diagnostic: he could decelerate *toward* her only in the safety of total isolation from his trigger-network (Wanda, Magneto, the Avengers, the wider world). The moment any trigger returned, his tempo did. Sustainable intimacy at speed has not been achieved in his record. Whether it is possible is an open empirical question.

**Dependency, hidden.** He is deeply dependent and presents as wholly autonomous. The dependency manifests as:
- Inability to function at full capacity outside team structures with clear chains of command. (X-Factor competence; freelance decompensation.)
- Recurrent need for Wanda's psychological proximity as baseline regulation. Long Wanda-absences correlate with his worst arcs.
- Substance-vulnerability (Terrigen) as displaced dependency need — when relational dependency cannot be met, chemical dependency substitutes.
- The pattern of bonding fast under depletion (Crystal). A genuinely autonomous person does not pair-bond at convalescence speed.

He cannot acknowledge the dependency because acknowledging it would collapse the narcissistic shell that defends the borderline core. So he denies it, and the denial drives the contempt — *I do not need you, you slow weak thing* is what he says to people he in fact desperately needs. The cruelty is the dependency speaking with the wrong vocabulary.

**Sexual / romantic register.** The available record is sparse and tightly controlled — Pietro is not depicted as promiscuous, not depicted as a seducer, and the Crystal marriage is the only fully developed romantic relationship in his canon. Read forensically, this is consistent with the attachment profile: a man with disorganized attachment and a fused twin-bond does not have a free-ranging erotic life. He has one woman at a time, in the rare moments he can have one at all, and the woman is asked to do the impossible work of being-not-Wanda-but-comparably-stable. The candidates fail not because they are inadequate but because the demand is incoherent.

---

## VII. THE RELATIONAL TEMPLATE — THE PATTERN REPEATED ACROSS EVERY RELATIONSHIP

This is the consolidated finding. Every Pietro relationship of consequence follows the same six-phase template, with only the durations and intensities varying. Sixty years of canon, one shape:

**Phase 1 — Approach in Contempt.** He enters with sneer, distance, dismissal. He tests whether the other will withdraw. Most do. The ones who do not, advance to Phase 2.

**Phase 2 — Rapid Bond Under Depletion or Necessity.** Once vetted minimally, he attaches with disproportionate speed and intensity, often during a moment of his own vulnerability (injury, isolation, defection-in-progress). The bond carries the weight of unmet attachment need accumulated over years.

**Phase 3 — Idealization.** The bonded person is briefly perfect — savior, partner, family, the answer. This phase is the shortest. It is also the only phase in which he is visibly happy.

**Phase 4 — Surveillance and Test.** Suspicion activates. He begins running covert diagnostics on the bond. Micro-tests of loyalty, monitoring of attention, alertness for any sign of the other turning toward someone or something else. The other party usually does not know they are being tested. They begin failing tests they were not informed of.

**Phase 5 — Splitting and Rupture.** A trigger fires — withdrawal, correction, a pattern-match to old betrayal, or a Wanda-coded threat. The bonded person is reclassified as enemy. The rupture is loud, public, and morally framed. He leaves *at* them. Depending on stress level, the rupture is a Resignation, a Vendetta-Construction, or in extreme cases a Reality-Rewrite or Substance-Betrayal.

**Phase 6 — Disappearance, Oblique Return, Slow Repair.** Months or years pass. He reappears at the margin. Service re-engages. Verbal apology, if it comes, is short. The relationship resumes in a damaged, vigilant register. The next cycle begins, sometimes years later, sometimes immediately.

**Where the template breaks.**
- **With Wanda**, the template does not complete because Phase 5 is structurally impossible — he cannot fully rupture from her because she *is* the substrate. So with her, the cycle truncates at Phase 4 (Surveillance and Test) and loops there indefinitely, with occasional flares toward Phase 5 (House of M) and Phase 6 (every quiet reconciliation since).
- **With Magneto**, Phase 3 (Idealization) is the only phase that ever resolves cleanly, and it is immediately followed by Phase 5 with no Phase 4 in between, because the trigger is the relationship itself — Magneto cannot help being Magneto, and so the rupture is structural. The cycle then resumes, *forever*, because Pietro cannot stop hoping.
- **With Luna**, the template is observably arresting itself. Phases 1 (Approach in Contempt) and 4 (Surveillance and Test) do not appear with her at all — she is the only intimate to whom he extends unconditional positive regard. Phase 5 occurred once, catastrophically, during Son of M. Phase 6 has been sustained and is, on the available evidence, holding. **Luna is the only relationship in his life in which the template appears to have been interrupted by his own deliberate choice.** This is the most important data point in his late record. It establishes that the pattern is not unbreakable — only that breaking it requires a love whose failure he cannot survive.

---

## VIII. SUMMARY OBSERVATION
