The framework was always capable of this; it had never been given the conditions.

**Phase 3 — First Decompensation Arc (1979 – c. 1985).** The Crystal betrayal collapses Phase 2. The code does not change; the *trust* that sustains it does. He returns to loyalty-only operation, now with paranoid sub-routines. Justification machinery (Section 7.4) develops here into its mature form.

**Phase 4 — X-Factor / Structured-Command Era (late 80s – mid 90s).** The Peter David period. Pietro discovers that external structure stabilizes his ethics. With a chain of command, a clear adversary, and explicit recognition of competence, he can hold the code without the decompensation cycles. He does not generalize from this discovery. He should have.

**Phase 5 — Magneto-Recognition Cycles and Luna's Childhood (mid 90s – 2005).** Ethical performance is increasingly contingent on the state of the Magneto relationship. Luna becomes the steady moral north — every decision he makes well during this period is made with Luna in view. The decisions made *without* Luna in view drift.

**Phase 6 — House of M and Son of M (2005 – 2007).** Total collapse. The framework is overwhelmed by the convergence of Wanda's breakdown, Magneto's failure to recognize him at Genosha, the M-Day depowering, and the Terrigen addiction. *Every* hard constraint except the explicit ones in Section 7.2 is breached. Luna is endangered. Wanda is manipulated into an act of world-historical harm. The Inhumans are betrayed. He cannot, after, account for himself.

**Phase 7 — Rehabilitation (2008 – present, through Mighty Avengers / Uncanny Avengers / All-New Inhumans).** The first genuine moral *development*, as opposed to oscillation. He acquires sustained self-awareness of the framework's failure modes. The apology to Luna is rendered. The attempt at apology to Wanda is attempted, repeatedly, with the difficulty he never grants himself for it. The hard constraints are now consciously held rather than tacitly operative — which makes them stronger against future stress and weaker against the next decompensation, because conscious holding is harder than reflex. He is, for the first time, a moral agent in the full sense: he can be asked why he did something, and the answer is not a rationalization but an attempt at one and a recognition that it is an attempt.

**The arc.** From inherited loyalty-ethics worn ill-fittingly, through structured competence, through catastrophic collapse, into the slow construction of a self-owned code that is still mostly the original loyalties but is now *chosen*. The content has barely moved. The relationship to the content has been remade.

---

## 7.7 — The Code Under Specific Pressures

A behavioral matrix, for operational use:

- **Under time pressure.** Code holds, sometimes better than at leisure — speed converts ethics to reflex, and his reflexes are mostly good. The hard constraints (Section 7.2) are most reliable here.
- **Under social pressure.** Code holds against peer pressure; fractures against authority pressure when the authority is Magneto-coded. The Magneto-shaped voice can move him to acts he would refuse from anyone else.
- **Under sexual / intimate pressure.** Code holds with striking firmness. The Crystal infidelity wounded him so deeply because his own fidelity was unquestioned. He does not stray. He does not abuse intimate access. The constraint is total.
- **Under threat to Wanda.** Code suspends almost entirely. This is the master fracture.
- **Under threat to Luna.** Code intensifies. The protective response is clean here in a way it is not with Wanda — Luna does not activate the abandonment terror; she activates the parental imperative. He is morally clearest when Luna is in view.
- **Under threat to self.** Code holds with indifference. He does not bargain when only his life is at stake. He bargains only when others depend on him surviving.
- **Under power loss.** Code fractures catastrophically. M-Day and the Terrigen arc are the demonstration. The somatic mutilation of depowering destabilizes everything, because the framework was partly held by the body that enacted it.
- **Under boredom / understimulation.** Code drifts. He becomes cruel in conversation, dismissive of obligations he would honor under pressure, impulsive in commitments he will break. The most underrated risk factor in his profile.
- **Under explicit recognition.** Code stabilizes. Being seen — accurately, respectfully, as himself rather than as a Magneto-derivative — produces some of his best behavior. The Cap-acceptance early in Avengers tenure is the model. He is one of the rare operators for whom *being trusted* is actively rehabilitative.

---

## 7.8 — Bottom Line

Pietro Maximoff operates from a code that he experiences as principled and that the record reveals as loyalty-structured, with a small set of genuinely inviolable constraints, a larger set of constraints that fracture under specific named pressures, and an elaborate justification apparatus that papers over the fractures in real time. The code's center of gravity has never moved: it is his sister, his daughter, the unpaid debt to the father he cannot have, and the few who have earned through endurance the right to be loved by him at his speed. He is not a man without ethics. He is a man whose ethics are organized by attachment rather than by principle, and who has spent his life mistaking the first for the second — until, in his most recent phase, he has begun, slowly and with the difficulty appropriate to the work, to know the difference.


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# UATU ANALYTICAL WORKUP — SUBJECT: PIETRO MAXIMOFF / "QUICKSILVER"
## Section 6 — Communications & Linguistic Profile

---

### 6.1 The Foundational Problem: Speech at the Wrong Speed

Every linguistic feature in the subject's profile descends from one neurological fact: he can think, articulate, and physically produce phonemes at multiples of conversational baseline, but he is forced — socially, professionally, in court, in the kitchen — to throttle down to the speed of the people listening. This is the linguistic equivalent of a concert pianist forbidden to use more than three fingers. Everything that sounds like *style* in his speech — the clipped phrasing, the impatience, the contempt, the over-precision — is partly a coping architecture built around this constraint.

He has, in effect, two registers of speech: **throttled** (what others hear) and **unthrottled** (the bursts he permits himself in private, in combat, or under sufficient emotional pressure that the governor slips). The throttled register is what 95% of his recorded interactions display. The unthrottled register is the diagnostic gold.

In throttled mode he sounds like a man holding his breath through every sentence. In unthrottled mode he sounds, briefly, like himself.

---

### 6.2 Diction and Lexical Profile

**Register baseline: elevated, slightly archaic, transatlantic.** He speaks with a vocabulary noticeably above the room — Latinate verbs where Anglo-Saxon ones would do (*"comprehend"* rather than *get*, *"requires"* rather than *needs*, *"sufficient"* rather than *enough*), formal subjunctives intact (*"were I to,"* *"had you asked"*), and full contractions resisted in moments of emphasis (*"I will not,"* *"you cannot,"* enunciated). Roma-Sokovian–accented English from a polyglot childhood, smoothed over decades in Anglophone teams; traces remain in vowel placement and the occasional preserved European cadence on negation and conditional clauses.

The elevated register serves two functions: (a) it is a real reflection of multilingual immigrant education — he reads at adult level in at least four languages and code-switches without performance; and (b) it is a status weapon. He has discovered that vocabulary intimidates faster than threats and is harder to punish him for using.

**Loanword tells.** Under stress or in private with family, he reverts: Spanish endearments to Luna (*mija*, *cariño*) inherited from his Latino lineage; Romani fragments in fury or in grief (*"prikaza"* — bad omen, ruin — appears in his private speech around catastrophic events); German technical vocabulary when discussing physics or tactics, learned from European scientific reading; occasional French dropped in to wound or to flirt. He does not announce these switches. They appear and disappear without translation, which is itself a tell — he speaks *at* you in another language to test whether you can keep up, and the test result reorganizes how he treats you.

**Words he overuses.** *"Slow"* in every conceivable metaphorical extension — slow thinking, slow understanding, slow to act, slow to admit, slow death. *"Already"* as a temporal accusation (*"I already said,"* *"you already know"*). *"Obvious"* and *"obviously"* as a prefatory contempt-marker that disclaims the need to explain. *"Adequate"* and *"sufficient"* as deliberately faint praise. *"Wanda"* — used as a sentence by itself, an explanation, a refusal, an apology, depending on intonation. The name does the work of paragraphs.

**Words he avoids.** *"Please"* in any non-ironic register, except to Luna. *"Help."* *"Afraid."* *"Wait"* — which he treats as an obscenity directed at his nervous system. *"Father"* unmarked — it is always *"my father,"* *"the man,"* *"Magneto,"* *"Erik,"* the article and the distance doing constant calibration work. *"Forgive"* — almost never offered, rarely requested. *"Love"* in the declarative — only to Luna in private; to Wanda only at extremity.

**Numbers and specificity.** He quantifies obsessively when calm — distances in meters not approximations, intervals in seconds and fractions, body counts and casualty windows precise. This is partly the sprinter's habit of measuring everything, partly a control mechanism: precision is a way of refusing the room's looser language.

---

### 6.3 Syntax: The Throttled Sentence

His sentences in conversation are characteristically **short, parsed, and grammatically complete.** He does not trail off. He does not um. He does not rephrase mid-clause. He composes the sentence at full speed inside his head and delivers it as a finished object — which produces the eerie effect, for interlocutors, of someone *reading* fluent speech rather than improvising it.

The downstream tells:

- **Almost zero filled pauses.** No *uh*, no *like*, no *you know*. The absence is conspicuous; people register him as unnaturally articulate or unnaturally rehearsed without being able to say why.
- **Parallelism under stress.** When agitated he falls into triadic constructions — *"You will not stop me, you will not slow me, you will not stand between us."* The triple is a tell that he has decompensated *up* into rhetoric rather than down into dysfluency. Most people get less articulate under pressure; he gets more.
- **The dropped subject.** In rapid exchange he amputates the subject pronoun — *"Already done,"* *"Don't care,"* *"Won't be there long,"* *"Told you."* This is his closest approach to genuine casualness, and it surfaces with people he has accepted.
- **The trailing barbed clause.** A declarative followed, after a beat, by an evaluative coda: *"The plan will work. — Assuming the rest of you can keep pace."* The coda is the contempt-delivery device. It appears late in the sentence so the listener has accepted the first half before the second half lands.
- **Hyperextended sentences in writing.** His written communication — emails, mission reports, the rare letter — runs to the opposite extreme: long, hypotactic, multiply subordinated, sometimes Jamesian in clause-stacking. Writing is the one medium where his speed is *not* constrained, so he luxuriates in it. A two-paragraph email from him reads like a brief.

---

### 6.4 Prosody, Pace, and the Tells of the Governor

The most diagnostic auditory feature: **his speech is faster than the room's, but evenly faster — not rushed.** He hits roughly 200+ words per minute in conversational baseline (standard American is ~150) and can clear 300 without losing articulation. He is not in a hurry; he is at *his* speed, which happens to be everyone else's hurry. People consistently describe being talked-at-fast even when he believes he is being patient.

**Throttling tells.** When he is forcing himself to slow down for someone he does not respect — a bureaucrat, a journalist, a slower teammate — the symptoms appear in the *pauses*, not the speech. Beats land in the wrong places. Brief silences gap mid-sentence where his mouth has gotten ahead of his permission to deliver the next word. The micro-expression that accompanies these is a tightening of the jaw and a single sharp inhalation through the nose — the body protesting the deceleration.

**The unthrottled burst.** Under combat conditions, on the comms during an operation, or in private fury, the governor drops. Two seconds of unfiltered speed: a paragraph delivered in the time most people produce a clause. Teammates report needing the recording slowed to follow it. He is, in those bursts, perfectly intelligible to himself, and forgets that others are not.

**Intonation range: narrow.** He does not vary pitch much. Sarcasm, sincerity, threat, and tenderness all live in a relatively compressed band, distinguished more by *word choice* and *timing* than by melody. This makes him hard to read for people accustomed to prosodic emotional cues — and produces frequent misreadings, particularly of his rare warmth, which sounds clinical because it is delivered in the same flat-rapid register as everything else.

**The Wanda exception.** When speaking to or about his sister, the rate drops noticeably — closer to 130 wpm, sometimes lower. Vowels lengthen. Pauses appear where, with anyone else, none would. This deceleration is the single most reliable affective tell in his entire vocal repertoire. If he slows down for you, he loves you. Almost no one else triggers it. Luna does. No one else.

**Accent migration under stress.** The smoothed transatlantic surface cracks under fatigue, grief, or rage; the European vowel placement returns, and Spanish/Romani phonotactics bleed through. Witnesses in House of M–adjacent moments describe him "sounding foreign again" — meaning the construction he has spent decades laminating onto his speech is the construction that comes off first when he breaks.

---

### 6.5 Register by Context

**With Wanda.** Lowest rate. Highest tenderness-per-word ratio. Bilingual without warning. Sentences sometimes begin in English and finish in Sokovian or Spanish. Permits himself fragments, sighs, and the unfinished thought — the only interlocutor with whom he does not need to compose the finished sentence in advance. Uses her name as a one-word complete utterance carrying any of: greeting, warning, apology, plea, prohibition, grief. Calls her *sestra* in extremity, never casually.

**With Luna.** The softest register he possesses. Diminutives, Spanish endearments, a near-musical cadence used nowhere else. Asks questions and waits for answers — a behavior almost absent from his interactions with adults. Repairs after failure with her are the only repairs he initiates without prompting; the language of those repairs is plain, short, and devoid of his usual ornament. *"I was wrong. I am sorry. I will do better."* No hedges, no Latinate cover.

**With Magneto.** The most distorted and revealing register. He oscillates within a single conversation between formal address (*"Father,"* offered like a test object), bitter honorific (*"Lord Magneto,"* heavy with quotation marks), and bare given name (*"Erik"*) deployed to wound. Sentence rate climbs above his own already-high baseline — the only person who can speed him up rather than force him to slow down. Pressured-speech phenomena appear: more interruption, more parallelism, more grandiose flourish. He is performing the son he wants Magneto to see while contesting the son Magneto wants him to be, in the same sentence.

**With Captain America (and equivalent legitimated authority).** Most controlled register. Clean diction, full sentences, near-military terseness, *"sir"* deployed sparingly and meant. Does not interrupt. Speaks when addressed. The throttling is conscious and visible — he respects this man and the language reflects discipline imposed from inside, not outside. The discipline cracks the moment he perceives condescension; one slip and he is out the door, mid-sentence.

**With Hawkeye (and similar mirror-image volatiles).** Most degraded register. Profane, jagged, personal. Drops the elevated vocabulary entirely; reaches for short Anglo-Saxon ugliness because Latinate distance is no longer worth the effort. The barbed coda becomes a barbed *opening*. Sarcasm goes feral. He hears himself in the other man and the language attacks the mirror.

**With Vision.** A specific, sustained register of icy formality, with intentional misuse of pronouns — *"it"* deployed surgically — and an over-precise diction that frames the synthezoid as object. He has, on rare occasions, slipped and called Vision *"he,"* which he treats as a defeat.

**With Crystal (historical) and other romantic objects.** A register no one else gets to hear at length, but the textual residue suggests an awkward courtly mode — formal endearments delivered with the same precision as a mission report. He does not have a natural language of romantic intimacy. He has *imported* one, mostly from European literature, and uses it stiffly.

**With teammates of accepted competence.** Clipped collegial mode. First names only. Short directives. The occasional dry compliment delivered as an aside — *"Adequate, Rogers"* — meant warmly and almost universally received as cold. He genuinely does not know how badly his warmth reads.

**With press, public, bureaucrats.** Maximally formal, maximally articulate, maximally throttled. The accent smooths to nothing. Sentences are pre-built. He will use the third person about himself (*"Quicksilver was not present at the engagement"*) to disclaim emotional content. Visibly miserable. Exits as fast as protocol permits.

**With himself (overheard private muttering, the diary fragments where they exist).** Multilingual stream, frequently in his Romani or Spanish substrate, frequently in second-person self-address (*"You should not have said that. You knew. You knew and you spoke anyway."*) — a tell of internalized scolding voice, likely Magneto-coded. Self-talk is harsher than anything he says aloud to others.

---

### 6.6 Rhetorical Strategies

**Preemption.** He opens conversations he expects to be hostile by stating the other person's argument first, dismantling it, and proceeding as if it had already been refuted. This is a speed-strategy applied to discourse: cover the predicted ground before the slower interlocutor gets there. Often effective. Often infuriating. Reads as bad faith even when it is not.

**The corrective interjection.** He interrupts to correct factual or grammatical errors, even small ones, even when they do not bear on the conversation. He does not experience this as rudeness; he experiences it as efficiency. The interlocutor experiences it as contempt. Both readings are correct.

**Argument by exhaustion.** When he wants to win, he buries the other side in volume — more clauses, more examples, more precise refutations than the slower mind can track. He is aware this is unfair and uses it anyway.

**The single-word demolition.** Conversely, when he wants to *end* an argument rather than win it, he deploys a one-word reply — *"No."* *"Enough."* *"Wanda."* — and leaves. The exit *is* the rhetoric.

**Sarcasm as primary mode.** Roughly 30–40% of his utterances in casual contexts carry sarcastic load. The sarcasm is dry, often missed, and rarely cruel by intent — but cumulatively corrosive. He uses it as a buffer against having to mean things.

**The historical reference.** When making serious points he reaches for examples drawn from European history, Romani persecution, mutant history, the witch-burning of medieval Europe — a referential repertoire that gives away both his education and his preoccupations. He never uses these references decoratively; they always carry argumentative weight, usually about persecution, betrayal, or the cost of complacency.

**Refusal of euphemism.** He says *killed*, not *lost*; *failed*, not *did our best*; *betrayed*, not *let down*. The bluntness is not a virtue, it is a refusal to spend the extra syllables on softening. He has been told this is cruel. He agrees and continues.

---

### 6.7 Deflection Language

The defense-architecture (splitting, intellectualization, contempt, projection) has specific linguistic fingerprints.

**Intellectualization.** When a feeling-question is asked, he answers with an analysis. *"How are you?"* → *"The mission parameters were satisfied."* *"Are you angry?"* → *"Anger would be an inefficient response."* The diagnostic move: the answer is *about* the topic but never *of* it.

**Contempt-deflection.** When pressed on his own behavior he reframes the question as evidence of the questioner's inadequacy. *"You are not equipped to understand."* *"This is not a productive conversation."* *"I will not justify myself to you."* The deflection is grammatical: the subject of the sentence shifts from him to the questioner mid-exchange.

**The third-person dodge.** Discussing his own decompensations, he frequently moves into the third person or the passive voice: *"Mistakes were made."* *"Quicksilver acted on incomplete information."* *"What was done cannot be undone."* The grammatical distance is exactly the emotional distance he needs to discuss the material at all.

**The pivot to action.** When a conversation threatens to remain in the affective register too long, he proposes a task. *"We should be moving."* *"There is work to do."* The pivot is so reliable that close associates use it as a thermometer: the moment he proposes motion, the conversation has touched something.

**Counter-accusation.** Under direct confrontation about his own failures, he reaches reflexively for the other's. *"And you — when you —"* This is the projective-identification mechanism in linguistic form. He sometimes catches himself doing it, sometimes does not. With Wanda, he catches himself. With Hawkeye, he never has.

**The exit-line.** When he cannot win and will not lose, he produces a finished, often quotable sentence and leaves before it can be answered. He composes these in advance — the speed advantage means he can pre-write his exit while the previous speaker is still in their first sentence. The exit-line is a tell of capitulation disguised as victory.

---

### 6.8 The Language of Love

He has almost no vocabulary for it and has built workarounds.

**To Luna.** Direct and small. *"Mija."* *"I am here."* *"You are safe."* *"I love you."* — said only to her, said often, said in the same plain mode every time. This is the only register in which he uses *love* as a verb in the first person without armor. The plainness is itself the love-signal: nowhere else is he this unornamented.

**To Wanda.** Indirect, ambient, behavioral-translated-into-speech. He does not say *I love you* to his sister. He says *Are you eating.* He says *Where are you.* He says *I am coming.* He says her name. The grammar of his love for her is the grammar of presence and supply: he names the conditions of her safety and reports his own location relative to her. When extremity forces a declaration, it is delivered in Sokovian or Romani, never in English — the foreign tongue providing the cover the feeling cannot otherwise survive.

**To teammates he loves (rare, real).** Dry compliment, the barbed coda inverted into a barbed *kindness* — *"You did not embarrass yourself, Rogers."* The form is contempt; the content is affection; the contradiction is the entire signal. Those who learn to read it learn to be grateful.

**To romantic partners.** Imported, stiff, often quoting. He has been heard to recite poetry to lovers. The recitation is sincere and embarrassing simultaneously.

---

### 6.9 The Language of Threat

**Direct mode.** Short, declarative, second-person, no modal hedging. *"You will not touch her."* *"You will stop now."* *"I will be there before you finish that sentence."* — and the last is sometimes literal. Threat in his mouth is *promise framed as forecast*, which is what gives it weight.

**Indirect mode.** Conditional with a temporal cap. *"If you do that, you will have approximately one second to reconsider."* The specificity of the time-interval is the threat; he is informing the target that he has measured exactly how long they will exist in their current configuration.

**The smile-threat.** A particular vocal-affect pattern where the rate slows (a Wanda-coded marker, deployed here as inversion) and the diction becomes elaborately polite. *"I would be obliged if you would explain that again, more carefully."* This is the most dangerous register he has — the throttling is voluntary, the politeness is performance, and the next thing that happens is usually not verbal.

**Silence-as-threat.** He uses pauses surgically. A speedster choosing to be still and silent in the middle of a conversation is making a statement about restraint, and the listener can feel it. He knows.

---

### 6.10 The Language of Grief

He does not have one in English. Grief in him produces:

- **Code-switch into Romani or Sokovian.** The Romani word *prikaza* — ruin, blight, bad-luck-coming — has been overheard at the loss of Wanda, the loss of his powers, the moment Crystal left. He does not translate it.
- **Numerical recitation.** He recites times, distances, intervals — *"Three minutes, forty seconds. I was three minutes and forty seconds away."* — converting grief into the only language his nervous system speaks fluently. Specificity is mourning.
- **Sudden refusal of speech.** Grief shuts him down rather than opening him up. He goes silent for hours or days and physically removes himself at speed. The absence is the keening.
- **Apology to the wrong person.** When grief catches him without a witness who can receive it, he apologizes to whoever is nearby. Subordinates have been thanked profusely for unrelated competencies in the wake of his losses. He is discharging affect into the closest available channel.
- **Rage as grief-substitute.** Most reliably, he converts. The funeral becomes a vendetta. The loss becomes a list of targets. Language of mourning becomes language of warning. This is the single most consistent post-loss linguistic shift in the record.

---

### 6.11 Honesty, Deception, and Tells

**Baseline: high honesty, low diplomacy.** He lies poorly because lying requires the slow patience of consistency-management, and he does not have it. He prefers refusal, evasion, or hostile truth.

**The deception tells.** When he does lie, the rate *drops* — he is composing carefully and the composition takes time even at his speed. He also shifts into the more elevated diction, the formal subjunctive, the over-precision. A sentence beginning *"It would not be accurate to say that —"* is almost always a lie wrapped in scrupulous grammar. Watch the verb choice; deception lives in his subordinate clauses, not his main ones.

**The omission tell.** He is a virtuoso of the technically-true selective answer. The thing he is hiding is usually structurally adjacent to what he just said — same topic, one frame over. He will answer the question literally asked and not the question meant. The tell is the *neatness* of the answer; his honest answers are messier.

**The tell he cannot suppress.** When he is lying about something that touches Wanda or Magneto, his eyes do a single rapid scan of the room — exits, distances, witnesses — before he answers. The scan is faster than most people can register, but it is there. He is preparing the body to leave because the mouth is doing something the body finds intolerable.

---

### 6.12 Written Communication

Long, formal, well-constructed, occasionally beautiful. Mission reports run to twice the expected length and contain editorial commentary in footnotes. Personal letters — rare — are composed with the care of someone who knows the recipient will read them more than once. Email response times are absurdly fast; he replies in seconds and is mildly insulted when others do not.

He keeps a journal, intermittently. Entries are dated to the minute. Handwriting is small, fast, and tightly controlled. Multilingual without internal translation. Tone in the journal is markedly harsher toward himself than any external speech permits; he uses second-person self-address (*"You knew better. You did it anyway."*) and the language of judgment in the journal is the language of the father he is trying not to become and cannot stop quoting.

---

### 6.13 Summary of Operational Tells

- *Slow rate of speech* = he loves you, fears you, or is lying.
- *Code-switch into Romani/Spanish* = the feeling has overflowed the English container.
- *Third-person self-reference* = decompensation discussed at the only distance he can t


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*Forecasts of subject behavior in granular, everyday, social, and low-stakes operational contexts the canon never depicts. Format: GIVEN condition → EXPECT response, with mechanism. High-confidence unless flagged.*

---

## A. WAKING, MORNING, DOMESTIC BASELINE

**GIVEN** an undisturbed night in his own quarters → **EXPECT** a wake time between 04:40 and 05:20, unprompted by alarm. Mechanism: the accelerated metabolism strips sleep architecture; he reaches REM saturation faster and wakes when the body has consumed its caloric reserve. He does not lie in bed. Feet on floor within four seconds of consciousness; standing within seven. The bed is remade before he has crossed the room — a single hand-sweep that is muscle memory, not tidiness.

**GIVEN** a hotel room, safehouse, or unfamiliar bed → **EXPECT** worse sleep, earlier waking (03:00–04:00), and a perimeter walk of the room before he sits down to anything. He will know where the exits are, where the HVAC vent is, where a person could stand outside the door. He logs this without articulating it.

**GIVEN** access to a kitchen first thing → **EXPECT** a four-to-six-thousand-calorie breakfast assembled in under two minutes: eggs (six to ten), whatever starch is fastest (toast, cold rice, plantains if he stocked them, oatmeal microwaved not simmered), a full pot of coffee drunk while standing, and a banana or two consumed in transit between counter and table. He eats fast but not messily — speed makes him *more* precise, not less. Plate goes in the sink, rinsed, before he sits.

**GIVEN** no kitchen → **EXPECT** a stash. He always has a stash: protein bars in jacket lining, an electrolyte sachet in a wallet pocket, dextrose tabs somewhere. He has hypoglycemia'd in the field once and will not do it twice.

**GIVEN** a mirror in the morning → **EXPECT** a glance, not a study. The silver hair he stopped processing as remarkable in his teens; he runs a hand through it rather than combing. The face he checks for one thing only — whether he looks tired enough that someone will comment. If yes, he will preempt with a sharper-than-usual opener to whoever sees him first.

**GIVEN** a shower → **EXPECT** under ninety seconds, water hot. He does not linger anywhere; lingering is a category his body resists.

---

## B. DRESS, GROOMING, SOMATIC PRESENTATION

**GIVEN** civilian dress → **EXPECT** a narrow palette: dark fitted clothing, technical fabrics that breathe and dry fast, running shoes or low trail-runners even with otherwise dressy outfits. Silver, gunmetal, black, occasional deep blue. Nothing loose at the wrists or ankles — drag at speed. Belt always cinched one notch tighter than looks comfortable. Watch on the left wrist, analog, because he likes seeing the second hand crawl.

**GIVEN** he must dress formally → **EXPECT** competence and visible discomfort. Suit cut close, jacket unbuttoned when seated, tie loosened within thirty minutes. He owns one suit, knows where it is, and resents needing it.

**GIVEN** a haircut decision → **EXPECT** he cuts it himself or has Wanda do it, never a barber he doesn't know. The silver invites questions he stopped answering at fifteen. Short faded sides, textured curls on top, kept tight enough that wind at full sprint does not catch it. Re-cut every nine to twelve days.

**GIVEN** facial hair → **EXPECT** clean-shaven most days, three-day stubble when he has been working a problem and forgot, never a beard. Shaving is fast and unceremonious — straight razor would be faster but he uses a multi-blade because the calculus of risk-vs-time tipped against the razor years ago after one mistake.

**GIVEN** scent → **EXPECT** nothing applied. He runs hot, sweats clean (high metabolic turnover, low bacterial load), showers often. Cologne is sensory clutter and a beacon. Deodorant unscented.

**GIVEN** jewelry → **EXPECT** none, with one possible exception: something small from Luna kept in a pocket, not worn. Anything on the body that can swing, catch, or shift weight asymmetrically at velocity is intolerable.

---

## C. MOVEMENT, GAIT, MICRO-LOCOMOTION

**GIVEN** he is walking at "normal" speed for company → **EXPECT** a gait that reads as relaxed but is in fact a deliberate, exhausting modulation. He takes shorter strides than his legs want, lands more heavily than he would at speed (the heel-strike of someone bored with the floor), and his hands either swing loose or, more often, go into pockets to suppress the urge to gesture-talk at conversational tempo.

**GIVEN** he is alone in a corridor → **EXPECT** speed snaps to a brisk jog at minimum, often a blur for the longer stretches, then dropped abruptly before any door he might be seen exiting. He polices the seam between his interior tempo and what others can witness.

**GIVEN** he stops moving entirely → **EXPECT** micro-motion: foot tap (almost inaudible, ball of the foot, not heel), finger drum against thigh or armrest, jaw shift, a pulse of weight transfer hip-to-hip. He is never still. Forced stillness (a long briefing, a flight, a meal at a slow table) produces increasingly visible tells.

**GIVEN** stairs → **EXPECT** always taken. Elevators are a confinement-and-wait combination he physically dislikes — he will take twenty flights up rather than ride. If forced into an elevator with others he stands closest to the door, weight forward.

**GIVEN** he must wait in a line, at a counter, in a lobby → **EXPECT** maximum thirty seconds of compliance before he is doing something else: pacing the perimeter, reading every posted notice, eavesdropping on adjacent conversations, going outside and coming back. Waiting reads to him as a small humiliation.

**GIVEN** sitting at a table → **EXPECT** the chair pushed back slightly farther than others', body angled toward the nearest exit by ten to fifteen degrees, one foot flat and one on the ball — a runner's set position disguised as posture.

**GIVEN** he is offered a ride somewhere → **EXPECT** polite refusal unless social cost of refusing exceeds the irritation of being driven. He drives himself or runs. If a passenger, he watches the road like a backseat driver and his foot ghost-brakes.

---

## D. SPEECH, CADENCE, VERBAL TICS

**GIVEN** ordinary conversation → **EXPECT** clipped sentences, dense information per breath, an accent that is mid-Atlantic-mutant-diaspora — neither fully Sokovian nor American, with Romance-language vowel residue that thickens when tired or angry. He elides articles when rushed ("Need the keys," "Saw it already"). His vocabulary is large and acidic; he reaches for the precise word and is annoyed when others reach for an approximation.

**GIVEN** he is interrupted → **EXPECT** he does not yield the floor — he speeds up, finishes the sentence at twice the rate, and *then* asks what the interruption was, with edge. He has been interrupted his entire life by people who can't keep up; the algorithm is hardwired.

**GIVEN** another person is speaking slowly → **EXPECT** visible suffering. Finger on his own knee tapping at the speaker's syllabic rate as if trying to push them. He may complete their sentence — correctly, three times out of four, which makes it worse. He has trained himself, marginally, to suppress this in formal contexts.

**GIVEN** small talk → **EXPECT** he doesn't. Greetings are functional: name, eye contact, one beat, business. If forced into pleasantry he is competent but visibly elsewhere. He does not ask "how was your weekend" and is offended on principle when asked, though he answers ("Fine.").

**GIVEN** he is genuinely interested in a person → **EXPECT** rapid-fire questions, real listening, and a memory for what they said that will surface six months later in a way that startles them. The contempt drops cleanly when curiosity engages. This is rare.

**GIVEN** he is being sincere → **EXPECT** he looks at the floor, the wall, the middle distance — anywhere but the listener's face. Earnestness costs him eye contact. The reverse of the cultural code; people who do not know him read this as evasion. It is the opposite.

**GIVEN** profanity → **EXPECT** sparing in English, freer in Spanish or his fractured Romani / Eastern-European phrasing when truly furious. Code-switches downward in register when alone with Wanda.

**GIVEN** he is being polite → **EXPECT** the politeness is correct, formal, and slightly nineteenth-century — the cadence of someone who learned manners as armor, not warmth. Strangers find it charming for ten minutes and chilly after thirty.

---

## E. EATING, NUTRITION, INTAKE

**GIVEN** a normal meal schedule → **EXPECT** five to seven feedings a day, not three. Two large, three to five tactical. He eats when the metabolic register demands and treats restaurant timing as a polite fiction.

**GIVEN** a restaurant with menus → **EXPECT** he chooses in under five seconds and then waits, drumming, while everyone else reads. He orders the highest-calorie protein-dense option and a side of carbohydrate, plus a second entrée if the portions look small. He will eat what others leave.

**GIVEN** a slow restaurant → **EXPECT** escalating irritation, eventual disappearance to "the bathroom" during which he eats a bar from his pocket, return with marginal patience restored.

**GIVEN** offered alcohol → **EXPECT** he accepts socially, drinks little, metabolizes it in minutes. Effective intoxication requires volumes that would kill a normal man. He does not drink to relax — he does not relax — and is wary of the Terrigen-shape of any substance-seeking impulse. Coffee is the exception: he drinks it constantly, less for the caffeine (which he barely registers) than for the ritual and the heat.

**GIVEN** cigarettes or drugs offered → **EXPECT** a hard, quick no. The Terrigen episode is the unspoken floor under every such offer. He does not explain the no.

**GIVEN** sweets → **EXPECT** preference for them, embarrassed about it. Dextrose burns clean in his system; pastries, chocolate, anything dense and sugary will be eaten standing over the box.

**GIVEN** dietary preferences of hosts → **EXPECT** he eats anything, complains about nothing at the table, and corrects misinformation about his needs *after* the meal, in private, with an edge. He hates being fussed over; he also hates being underfed.

---

## F. SLEEP, REST, DOWNTIME

**GIVEN** a sixteen-hour day with normal exertion → **EXPECT** four to five hours of sleep, sufficient. He has not slept eight hours uninterrupted since adolescence and does not believe people who claim to.

**GIVEN** sleep onset → **EXPECT** ten to thirty minutes of restlessness, often with a book or a screen — not for content, for the visual occupation that lets the mind decelerate. He reads quickly, finishes a novel in a sitting, retains structure better than detail.

**GIVEN** disturbed sleep → **EXPECT** he is up, dressed, and outside in under sixty seconds. He does not lie in bed thinking.

**GIVEN** a night when he cannot sleep at all → **EXPECT** a long run — twenty to two hundred miles depending on terrain and how much he is avoiding. He returns at dawn, eats massively, showers, works the day. This is his most reliable self-medication and the closest he comes to meditation. He will not call it that.

**GIVEN** "downtime" imposed by command or injury → **EXPECT** he is the worst patient in any infirmary. He will leave the bed within the hour, be retrieved, leave again, be threatened with sedation, comply for ninety minutes, attempt to leave again. Bedrest is a form of torture for him; the still body amplifies every interior signal he runs from.

**GIVEN** a vacation → **EXPECT** he doesn't take them. If forced (Wanda, Luna), he packs running shoes and disappears for hours at a time. He returns with reports on the local geography that no one asked for.

---

## G. WORK, OPERATIONS, STRUCTURED TASKS

**GIVEN** a structured task with clear parameters → **EXPECT** completion at multiples of expected pace, to spec, with sardonic commentary in the after-action. He thrives under explicit objectives, hates open-ended brainstorming.

**GIVEN** a meeting → **EXPECT** he is on time to early, sits near a door, contributes precisely once or twice with the most efficient possible articulation of what others are circling, and then visibly checks out. If the meeting exceeds forty minutes he will find an excuse to leave.

**GIVEN** he is asked to brainstorm → **EXPECT** discomfort and either over-contribution (rapid-fire ideas, some excellent, some half-formed, defended too hard) or withdrawal. He does not enjoy the iterative slow build.

**GIVEN** paperwork → **EXPECT** he does it, fast, accurately, and resents it the entire time. Handwriting is small, slanted, surprisingly legible. Signature is a slash.

**GIVEN** a deadline at distance → **EXPECT** procrastination is impossible — he completes early to clear the channel and then is irritated that others have not. The waiting between completion and others' completion is its own ordeal.

**GIVEN** a slow-moving project → **EXPECT** he disengages, finds parallel work, and returns when there is something to do. He is a poor sustainer of long latency tasks and knows it.

**GIVEN** he is asked to mentor or train → **EXPECT** he is *better* at it than expected. He can articulate the mechanics of speed and combat with surprising patience for the technical part; he is harsh on excuses and gentle on honest failures. He prefers training children to adults — they don't perform competence at him.

**GIVEN** subordinate failure → **EXPECT** sharp correction in private, public defense of the subordinate to outsiders. He runs his teams the way he wished he had been led.

---

## H. FAMILY — WANDA

**GIVEN** any room contains Wanda → **EXPECT** he locates her on entry, holds peripheral awareness of her continuously, and recalibrates posture relative to her position throughout. This is involuntary and present even when they are on poor terms.

**GIVEN** a phone call from Wanda → **EXPECT** he answers within two rings, every time, regardless of context. He has interrupted combat for it. He will not say "I have to call you back" — he will manage both.

**GIVEN** Wanda is upset → **EXPECT** he is at her location within whatever time the geography permits, before she has asked. He frequently mistimes this — arrives when she wanted space — and they fight about it predictably.

**GIVEN** a stranger speaks to Wanda dismissively → **EXPECT** verbal evisceration calibrated to the offense, delivered in front of her whether she wants it or not. He has not yet learned to ask first.

**GIVEN** she asks him not to intervene → **EXPECT** visible struggle, partial compliance, and a subsequent quiet correction of the situation she would not approve of if she knew. He believes she does not need to know.

**GIVEN** they have not spoken in weeks → **EXPECT** he is the one who breaks first, with a pretext (Luna, a logistical question, a forwarded link) rather than a direct overture. Direct emotional approach is harder than rebuilding a bridge.

---

## I. FAMILY — LUNA

**GIVEN** Luna in his presence → **EXPECT** his pace drops by half, voice softens by an octave, irritability vanishes for as long as she is in the room. The transformation is so total that teammates who witness it for the first time stare.

**GIVEN** scheduled custody or visit → **EXPECT** he is early, prepared, has researched whatever she is currently interested in, has snacks she likes, has cleared his schedule with paranoid completeness. He will not let work interrupt time with her if there is any way to prevent it.

**GIVEN** she asks about Crystal → **EXPECT** neutral-to-warm framing of her mother, with effort. He will not make her carry his grievances.

**GIVEN** she asks about his powers, the Terrigen incident, the things he did → **EXPECT** honesty in age-appropriate fragments. He will not lie to her. He has decided this and held it.

**GIVEN** she is in any danger → **EXPECT** the most controlled, lethal, decisive version of him in the entire behavioral repertoire. Speed without affect. Other parents would not recognize themselves.

**GIVEN** Luna disappoints him → **EXPECT** he does not show it, processes it elsewhere, returns having decided it was nothing.

---

## J. FAMILY — MAGNETO

**GIVEN** the name is mentioned → **EXPECT** a half-second of nothing, then either a sharp redirect or a too-casual response that fools no one. The half-second is the tell.

**GIVEN** Magneto is in the same building → **EXPECT** he knows it before being told, runs the room's exits, and either seeks contact or actively avoids it depending on which one feels more like a choice in the moment. There is no neutral.

**GIVEN** Magneto offers approval → **EXPECT** he accepts it visibly stiffly, drinks it greedily in private, and pre-emptively prepares for it to be withdrawn.

**GIVEN** Magneto criticizes him → **EXPECT** he absorbs without rebuttal, walks out within minutes, and the next decision he makes will be partly a refutation of the criticism whether or not he admits it.

**GIVEN** someone calls him "Magneto's son" with respect → **EXPECT** a brief, almost grateful flicker, then a deflection: "Wanda's brother, mostly."

**GIVEN** someone calls him "Magneto's son" with implication → **EXPECT** the temperature drops. He will not raise his voice. He will, somehow, end the conversation.

---

## K. SOCIAL — STRANGERS, ACQUAINTANCES, TEAMMATES

**GIVEN** introduction to a new person → **EXPECT** a fast handshake, eye contact held one beat longer than comfortable (assessment, not warmth), name registered and filed, immediate categorization on a fast/slow axis that he uses for the rest of the relationship.

**GIVEN** a teammate complains about him → **EXPECT** he hears about it (he hears about everything), confronts them within hours, and either resolves it sharply or files them in the permanent-distrust column.

**GIVEN** a teammate compliments him → **EXPECT** awkwardness disguised as dismissal: "It was nothing." He files the compliment forever.

**GIVEN** a teammate is in trouble → **EXPECT** he is there before the call ends. Loyalty in the operational register is total; the messiness is all in the relational register.

**GIVEN** romantic interest from a stranger → **EXPECT** he sees it before they have finished signaling, decides within seconds, and either declines cleanly or leans in with intensity that startles them. Middle gears are not available.

**GIVEN** a teammate's partner or child in his orbit → **EXPECT** he is unexpectedly gentle with children, formal-to-stiff with partners, and remembers their names and details with a precision that surprises everyone, including him.

**GIVEN** a social gathering, party, ceremony → **EXPECT** he arrives, makes the required circuit at high efficiency, finds a corner with a wall behind him, eats more than seems possible from the buffet, leaves at the earliest non-rude moment. He is the first one out unless Wanda is the host.

**GIVEN** he is asked to dance → **EXPECT** competent, fast, brief. He learned formally somewhere. He will not stay for a second song.

---

## L. TECHNOLOGY, ENVIRONMENT, OBJECTS

**GIVEN** any device with a loading bar → **EXPECT** profanity, force-quits, percussive maintenance. Latency is the universal enemy.

**GIVEN** he learns a new piece of equipment → **EXPECT** mastery in a single session, often by ignoring the manual and pressing every button in sequence at speeds that test the firmware.

**GIVEN** a phone → **EXPECT** screen at maximum refresh, predictive text disabled (slower than typing for him), notifications mostly off, three or four contacts on emergency override (Wanda, Luna, current team handler, one other), browser history aggressively cleared.

**GIVEN** music → **EXPECT** wide and idiosyncratic taste — high BPM electronic for runs, classic soul and salsa at home, classical when he wants to think, hip-hop he keeps quieter around teammates because he does not want to discuss it. The tastes were shaped early and he does not chase the new.

**GIVEN** his living space → **EXPECT** sparse, organized, clean by virtue of speed not discipline. Few decorations. Books on shelves alphabetized by author (he did it in three minutes once and has maintained it). A framed photo of Luna. Possibly nothing of Wanda visible — he does not need a photo, he has her in his head.

**GIVEN** weather → **EXPECT** he runs in all of it. Cold he prefers; the body's overheat in summer is a real constraint and he will be irritable in heat above thirty Celsius.

**GIVEN** a city he doesn't know → **EXPECT** mapped on foot within two hours of arrival. He cannot tolerate not knowing a place's exits.

---

## M. MICRO-TELLS, SOMATIC SIGNATURE, INVOLUNTARY DATA

**GIVEN** he is lying → **EXPECT** he is *better* at it than most, but the tell is overcontrol: he goes too still, the perpetual micro-motion drops out for the duration of the lie. Reading him requires knowing his baseline of motion.

**GIVEN** he is genuinely afraid → **EXPECT** he gets *quieter* and *faster*, not louder. Speech tightens to single words. The body moves to maximum readiness without his volition.

**GIVEN** he is grieving → **EXPECT** he is not where you can find him. He runs. He returns having processed enough to function and not enough to be reached on the topic.

**GIVEN** he is in physical pain → **EXPECT** he does not say so. The metabolism manages most of it. He will favor a limb almost imperceptibly; he will refuse analgesics that slow him.

**GIVEN** he is sick → **EXPECT** it is short (the metabolism burns viruses fast) and he is impossible during it. The body unaccustomed to weakness rebels against the experience.

**GIVEN** he is hungry


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*High-stakes behavioral forecasting. Each entry: a GIVEN antecedent (the situation, stimulus, or pressure), an EXPECT consequent (the predicted Pietro-specific response, with granular somatic, verbal, tactical, and decompensation-edge detail), and where useful a SECONDARY (the delayed second-order behavior, typically 24–72 hours later, after the first reaction has cooled into shame or hardened into vendetta). All predictions derive from the longitudinal record (Section 1) and the defense architecture (Sections 3–4). Confidence ratings are operator-grade, not clinical.*

---

## A. THE WANDA AXIS — Threats to the Twin Bond

This is the highest-priority predictive cluster. Wanda is the only continuously secure attachment object; any perturbation activates the disorganized-attachment substrate and overrides every other operating parameter, including self-preservation, mission discipline, and stated loyalties.

**GIVEN:** Wanda is physically endangered in his presence — hostage, ambushed, injured in front of him.
**EXPECT:** Sub-second tactical collapse of all standing orders. He will breach formation, break cover, ignore comms, abandon assigned objectives. Speed will spike past sustainable thresholds (he will burn calories he does not have to spare; expect tremor, tunnel vision, and hypoglycemic crash within 4–9 minutes of sustained max-output). Verbalization narrows to two-word imperatives shouted at whoever is between him and her. He will kill if he reads the threat as lethal, and he will not deliberate. The classic somatic tell: jaw locks, the silver hair flattens with sweat, and his hands — usually in motion — go *still* for the half-second before the sprint.
**SECONDARY (12–48 hours):** If she survived, he does not leave the room she is in. Sleeps in a chair, or does not sleep. If she did not, expect immediate vendetta-construction with a named target list within 24 hours, sustained for weeks. He will not eat at normal intervals. He will refuse all debriefs.
**Confidence:** Very high. This pattern is invariant across 60 years of canon.

**GIVEN:** Wanda is psychologically endangered — manipulated, gaslit, having a breakdown, in the grip of a power-spiral.
**EXPECT:** Different topography than physical threat. He becomes *quiet*, which is the diagnostic anomaly — Pietro is never quiet. He hovers within line-of-sight, speaks to her in a register no one else hears him use (slower, lower, almost gentle), and begins building plans that include other people without telling those people they are part of plans. House of M is the precedent: when he cannot fix her by being near her, he will conscript reality itself. Expect him to approach the most powerful entity in his Rolodex (a god-tier teammate, a cosmic artifact, his father) and propose something the entity will find horrifying. He will frame it as her idea.
**SECONDARY:** If anyone external "helps" her in a way he did not authorize, that person is converted to enemy-category within 72 hours regardless of outcome quality. Gratitude is not in the available register; the only acceptable helper is himself.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Wanda forms a new romantic or primary attachment (synthezoid, mutant, human, anyone).
**EXPECT:** Phase one — overt disgust framed as protectiveness ("he is not what you think," "she is using you," "this is beneath you"). The disgust will use whatever vocabulary is locally available; the *content* is irrelevant, the *function* is to interpose himself. Phase two — surveillance behavior. He will know the partner's schedule, vulnerabilities, financial history, and prior romantic record within a week, and will not have meant to. Phase three — a manufactured crisis that requires Wanda to choose. Phase four — if she chooses the partner, withdrawal and a self-destructive arc (substance-coded, mission-coded, or romantic-coded — the Crystal marriage is the canonical example of phase four converted into a counter-attachment).
**SECONDARY:** Long-term grudging tolerance is possible *only* if the partner survives a crisis Pietro witnesses them survive without him. He respects durability; he cannot respect anyone he has not seen bleed.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Wanda criticizes him directly — names a failure, sets a boundary, expresses fear of him.
**EXPECT:** The one input that does not trigger contempt. He goes still, the speed-baseline drops perceptibly (people who have only seen him at velocity find this uncanny), and he absorbs the criticism without immediate defense. He will then disappear for between four hours and three days. Whereabouts during the disappearance: physically exhausting solo movement, often running until the body forces a stop. Returns offering nothing verbal — instead, an action that constitutes the apology (a task done, a person retrieved, a threat removed).
**SECONDARY:** The criticism will be metabolized but never explicitly acknowledged. If she raises it again later, he will be irritable, because to him it was *handled*.
**Confidence:** Very high. Wanda is the only person whose criticism does not activate splitting.

**GIVEN:** Wanda chooses someone else's counsel over his in a high-stakes decision.
**EXPECT:** Visible flinch (microsecond; most observers miss it). Verbal compliance, sometimes performatively gracious. Then immediate parallel-track action: he will execute his preferred plan in the background while letting hers proceed officially. Discovery of the parallel track produces the first real fight; second-order rupture risk is high.
**Confidence:** High.

---

## B. THE MAGNETO AXIS — The Father Wound

The second-priority cluster. Magneto is the only stimulus that reliably overrides Wanda-priority, because Wanda-protection and Magneto-approval are organized in the same neural substrate and frequently demand contradictory action.

**GIVEN:** Magneto enters the operational theater unannounced.
**EXPECT:** A 30–90 second window of behavioral suspension — Pietro will be slower for the first minute after sighting than he has been in years, because the cognitive load of running the entire father-algorithm in foreground consumes processing normally allocated to motion. Speech becomes either clipped to the point of monosyllable or pressured to the point of overflow; there is no middle register available. Posture changes: he squares to Magneto's body, mirrors stance unconsciously, and stands closer than social distance allows. He will say something deliberately wounding within five minutes. He will fail to leave the room.
**SECONDARY:** Within 24 hours, one of three outcomes — (i) explicit alliance offered then rescinded, (ii) explosive denunciation followed by physical departure, (iii) silent absorption into Magneto's orbit for days or weeks. The path taken is determined by whether Wanda is also present and what *she* signals.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Magneto offers paternal approval — explicit, in words, witnessed.
**EXPECT:** This is the most dangerous predictive cell in the entire dossier. Pietro's defenses are not configured for *receiving* what he wants. Expect: visible destabilization (eyes wet, breath caught, the silver-haired head dropped fractionally), followed within minutes by an attack on the giver. The attack will be verbal, will be cruel, will be specifically calibrated to wound Magneto in his vanities, and will be incomprehensible to bystanders. He is testing whether the approval survives provocation. If it does, he will be useless to any other authority for the next 48–72 hours. If it does not (and historically it does not), he will treat the entire exchange as proof he was right to mistrust it, and the wound deepens one layer.
**SECONDARY:** Substance-vulnerability re-activates here. The Terrigen pattern is most likely to recur in the wake of a failed Magneto-approval cycle, not in the wake of physical loss.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Anyone calls him "Magneto's son" in a tone he reads as identification rather than respect.
**EXPECT:** Instant cold register. Speed drops to baseline-still (he weaponizes stillness; people who know him recognize it as the most dangerous mode). The reply will be one sentence, surgically chosen, designed to make the speaker regret the phrasing for years. If a stranger: this is the entire interaction; Pietro will not engage further. If a teammate: a multi-week cooling period in which the teammate is functionally invisible to him. If said by Magneto himself in possessive register ("my son"): see preceding cell — destabilization followed by attack.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Magneto is killed, captured, or publicly humiliated by a third party.
**EXPECT:** Counter-intuitive response. The third party is not the primary target — the *bystanders who failed to prevent it* are. Pietro will turn first on whoever was nearest Magneto in the moment, regardless of culpability, because the available rage is too large for the actual perpetrator alone. Then, after 12–48 hours, a vendetta against the perpetrator that will absorb him completely, with no concern for jurisdictional, legal, or tactical sense. If Magneto died: a period of grief that looks nothing like grief — productivity spike, contempt spike, refusal to attend any service, presence at the grave alone at 4 a.m. unwitnessed.
**Confidence:** High.

**GIVEN:** A father-figure substitute (Captain America, the team leader, a senior mentor) attempts paternal positioning.
**EXPECT:** Tested immediately and repeatedly. The tests are mostly verbal — disrespect calibrated to provoke. If the substitute holds ground without retaliation *and* without condescension, Pietro will accept the relationship within weeks, though he will never name it. If the substitute retaliates, the relationship ends. If the substitute condescends ("I understand you've had a hard time"), the relationship ends *and* converts to active hostility. The Cap relationship in the early Avengers run is the working model: respect grudgingly earned, never spoken.
**Confidence:** Very high.

---

## C. BETRAYAL — Real, Perceived, and Manufactured

**GIVEN:** A trusted intimate breaks confidence, lies to him, or is discovered to have withheld information.
**EXPECT:** No graduated response. The splitting defense activates instantly and the intimate is reclassified from saviour-category to betrayer-category in a single cognitive step. Verbal denunciation within minutes, often public, often disproportionate. Physical departure from the shared space within the hour. He will not return calls, will not accept apologies, will not attend mediated reconciliation for *months*. The Crystal precedent is governing: a single confirmed affair ended a marriage and produced a multi-year psychotic-edge spiral. Magnitude of the original betrayal is a poor predictor of magnitude of response; *trust differential* is the predictor — the more trusted, the more catastrophic.
**SECONDARY (weeks to years):** Oblique attempts at re-contact, framed as operational necessity. Never opens with apology; opens with a task. If the intimate accepts the task and performs it competently, repair becomes possible. If they demand a verbal apology first, repair is foreclosed for that cycle.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** He *suspects* betrayal without evidence.
**EXPECT:** Confirmation bias at speed. His cognitive style — premature closure on hypotheses, especially paranoid ones — means the suspicion hardens into conviction within hours. He will begin acting on the conviction before investigating it. Investigation, when it occurs, will be selective and will favor confirming data. Bystanders attempting to provide disconfirming information will be reclassified as colluding with the suspected betrayer. This is the mechanism by which a single misread glance metastasizes into the 1979–80 Avengers vendetta arc.
**Mitigation window:** Roughly the first 30–90 minutes after suspicion forms, *only* if the source of disconfirmation is Wanda. No other voice penetrates.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** An institutional betrayal — the team, the government, an organization he serves disowns or scapegoats him.
**EXPECT:** Less destabilizing than personal betrayal, because he expects it. Response is cold rather than hot: resignation delivered in writing or via abrupt departure, no scene, no monologue. He may then weaponize his knowledge of the institution against it — leaks, exposure, parallel operations — but without the manic affect of personal-betrayal response. The institutional betrayal *confirms* his operating model, which produces a paradoxical stabilization. He is at his most lucid in the aftermath of being betrayed by a system he never fully trusted.
**Confidence:** High.

**GIVEN:** He is asked to betray someone — turn informant, sell out a teammate, leverage Wanda against Magneto or vice versa.
**EXPECT:** The asker is converted to enemy-category instantly if the ask touches Wanda. For other targets, surface compliance is *possible* — Pietro can run a deception convincingly — but he will reroute the operation to preserve the target while appearing to deliver them. The pattern: he will *seem* to comply, then engineer an outcome in which the betrayal fails by "circumstance." If pressed about the failure, he becomes contemptuous. Direct accusation of double-cross is denied with rage proportional to its accuracy.
**Confidence:** High.

---

## D. TEMPTATION — Substance, Power, Reality-Editing

**GIVEN:** Access to a power-restoration or power-amplification substance (Terrigen, an unstable artifact, an experimental enhancement).
**EXPECT:** The Son of M arc is the diagnostic template and the vulnerability is permanent. First exposure may be framed as instrumental — "I need this for the mission" — but the addiction topography reactivates: tolerance escalation within days, increasing concealment, willingness to involve others in supply (and yes, including Luna if the floor drops out completely). Behavioral signs: secrecy disproportionate to the stakes, defensive irritability when the substance is mentioned, post-use crash periods during which he is unreachable, somatic markers (the silver hair brightens to near-white during use cycles; the skin loses its warm undertone and takes on grey at the temples and around the eyes).
**Window of intervention:** The first private use. After the second, the trajectory is established and only a catastrophic external event (Wanda's direct intervention, Luna's exposure to the substance, near-death) interrupts it. Verbal intervention by anyone other than Wanda or Luna is counter-productive — it accelerates use as defiance.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Offered a permanent power upgrade with a moral cost (kill X to gain Y, accept this dark-aligned source, become the avatar of this entity).
**EXPECT:** Surface refusal, real consideration. He will perform indignation and then think about the offer for days. The deciding variable is not the moral cost — it is whether accepting would *prove something to Magneto* or *protect Wanda*. If either, the moral cost shrinks; if neither, the offer is refused. The middle case (it would prove him to Magneto but cost a teammate) produces the worst paralysis and the highest risk of impulsive acceptance under fatigue.
**Confidence:** High.

**GIVEN:** Access to reality-editing capacity (cosmic artifact, ally with reality-warp power, time-travel option to undo a loss).
**EXPECT:** The House of M cell. This is the single most dangerous predictive scenario in the file. The grandiose-omnipotent-reparation defense activates and overrides every other operating parameter including Wanda-protection (because reality-editing is *framed* as her protection). He will not consult. He will not deliberate. He will engineer the change and present it as fait accompli. The intervention window is *before he knows the capacity exists*. After he knows, he is operating in a domain his decision-making cannot handle.
**Mitigation:** The only known stabilizer is Wanda explicitly forbidding it, in his presence, while regulated. Even then, confidence is moderate.
**Confidence:** Very high (for the pattern), moderate (for any mitigation).

**GIVEN:** Offered the leadership of a movement, team, or faction in which he would be the explicit Magneto-successor.
**EXPECT:** Accepts, with surface humility he does not feel. Performs the role competently for a defined period (weeks to months). Then a precipitating event — usually a subordinate's failure or a public comparison to his father — produces explosive abdication. He will not transfer the role gracefully; he will burn the office on his way out. The X-Factor leadership period is the counter-example: he held the role for an extended run because the structure was external (government-imposed) rather than self-claimed; he is better at *occupying* authority than *being* authority.
**Confidence:** High.

---

## E. THE SLOWING — Threats to Speed-Identity

**GIVEN:** He is depowered, even temporarily.
**EXPECT:** M-Day is the precedent and the response was Son of M. Depowering is processed as *amputation of self*, not loss of capacity. First 24 hours: denial, repeated attempts to access the power, confusion when it does not respond. 24–72 hours: rage, isolation, refusal to be seen by anyone who knew him at speed. Week one onward: search for restoration by any available means, ethical or not. He cannot tolerate the subjective experience of human-baseline time perception; what was background hum becomes deafening silence. Suicidality is non-trivial here; he will not name it but operators should watch for unnecessary risk-taking in the second and third weeks.
**Mitigation:** Sustained presence of Wanda and/or Luna, structured tasks within human-baseline capacity that he can still perform with excellence (analysis, strategy, language work — his cognitive speed survives somatic depowering). Without these, trajectory is catastrophic.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** A faster speedster appears — younger, more powerful, or simply newer.
**EXPECT:** Phase one: contempt and dismissal ("a child," "untrained," "a parlour trick"). Phase two: covert observation, careful study of the rival's technique, calibration of his own against theirs. Phase three: a manufactured competition, framed as instructional or operational, in which he intends to demonstrate primacy. Phase four-A: if he wins, contempt softens into grudging interest, and the rival may be apprenticed (he is capable of mentorship when the student acknowledges his primacy). Phase four-B: if he loses, splitting activates, the rival is converted to enemy-category, and a vendetta of variable duration follows. The risk-stratifying variable is *witnesses* — defeat without witnesses can be metabolized; defeat in front of Wanda, Magneto, or a team is much harder.
**Confidence:** High.

**GIVEN:** Aging or somatic degradation begins to manifest — slower recovery, joint wear, the speed becoming costly.
**EXPECT:** Concealment, first. He will not disclose. Compensatory technique refinement — he will run smarter as he can no longer run harder, and this is one of the rare zones where pressure produces growth rather than decompensation, because *he loves the craft of his power* and is willing to learn it deeper rather than louder. The crisis comes only when he cannot conceal the change from himself any longer — and the response then is a regression toward substance temptation (see Section D).
**Confidence:** Moderate-high.

**GIVEN:** Someone tells him to "slow down" or "calm down" in earnest.
**EXPECT:** A reflex contempt so reliable it can be used to identify him in a crowd. The phrase is the verbal correlate of every patronizing teacher, every slower opponent who could not keep up, every authority that asked him to be less. The response is calibrated to the speaker: stranger gets a glare and dismissal; teammate gets a barbed retort; intimate gets the cold register and a 12-hour withdrawal. The phrase from Wanda is the exception — from her, it is processed as request, not injury.
**Confidence:** Very high.

---

## F. LUNA — The Inverse Pressure Point

**GIVEN:** Luna is endangered.
**EXPECT:** Topographically distinct from the Wanda-endangered response. Slower, colder, more strategic. Luna activates the *higher-functioning* Pietro — the one who knows what kind of father he has been and what kind he is trying to become. He will plan rather than charge, coordinate rather than unilateralize, and ask for help (the only situation in which he reliably asks). The somatic tell: instead of stillness-then-sprint, he becomes verbally precise, full sentences, conditional clauses he never uses elsewhere.
**SECONDARY:** Sustained presence with her after the crisis — days, not hours. He will cancel obligations without explanation. Anyone who criticizes the cancellation is converted to enemy-category permanently.
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Luna names a failure of his as a father — directly, in her own voice, at any age.
**EXPECT:** The only stimulus in his entire behavioral universe that produces clean, immediate, unguarded apology. No splitting, no contempt, no rupture, no delay. The wound is too central, the guilt too earned, the defenses are not configured to deflect from her. He will accept the criticism, hold it, and attempt — usually clumsily — to act differently. This is the *one* leverage point through which sustained behavior change has historically been possible. Operators noting this should also note: it works once or twice. Repeated invocation by Luna risks her experiencing the dynamic as her burden to carry, which Pietro, when he perceives it, will not tolerate (he will withdraw to prevent her from being responsible for him, and the cycle resets).
**Confidence:** Very high.

**GIVEN:** Luna is used as leverage against him by an adversary.
**EXPECT:** The adversary has made a category error from which they will not recover. Pietro will exhaust every legitimate option *and then* every illegitimate one. There is no negotiation register here, no splitting register, no apology register. The behavior is goal-locked, sustained, and unbounded by prior alliance or law. Allies attempting to restrain him will be considered obstacles. The outcome for the adversary, if Pietro reaches them, is total.
**Confidence:** Very high.

---

## G. DECOMPENSATION SIGNATURES — Pre-Break Markers

Operators monitoring for the onset of a discrete psychotic-register episode (1979 Avengers vendetta, House of M, Son of M templates) should watch for the following clustering. Any two suggest elevated risk; any four suggest break is imminent or underway.

1. **Speech-rate inversion.** Pietro normally speaks at the upper bound of intelligibility. Pre-break, the speech *slows* — he becomes deliberate, almost formal, choosing words. This is the rarest and most diagnostic marker. The deceleration is not calm; it is the cognitive resource-reallocation toward an elaborate internal construction (the vendetta plan, the reality-edit, the supply scheme).

2. **Sleep collapse.** Mutant metabolism allows him to operate on minimal sleep


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 9
## VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM
### Subject: Pietro Maximoff ("Quicksilver")

---

> **Operator's preface.** This compendium is written for those who would *protect* the subject from himself and from those who would weaponize him — and, secondarily, for those who must work with him under conditions where misreading him produces casualties. Every lever described here is reversible: each pressure point is also a tending-point, each provocation also a soothing. The same channels that destabilize him are the channels through which he is reached. Read both columns of every entry.

---

## I. THE PRIMARY VULNERABILITY MATRIX

There are exactly **four** load-bearing wounds in this man. Everything else is a sub-circuit of one of them. List them in order of catastrophic potential:

1. **Wanda.** The twin-bond. The only continuous secure attachment of his life. Pressure here produces the largest and most unpredictable responses in the dossier.
2. **Magneto.** The unhealed paternal wound. Pressure here produces the most *predictable* responses — the algorithm is fixed, only the amplitude varies.
3. **Speed / extraordinariness.** The compensatory identity. Pressure here produces the fastest collapse from functional to dangerous, because it strikes the defense itself.
4. **Luna.** The reparative attachment. The *only* pressure point that, when correctly engaged, produces *better* behavior rather than worse. Mishandled, it produces the deepest shame in his repertoire — and shame is the affect he tolerates least.

Everything below organizes around these four.

---

## II. WANDA — THE LOAD-BEARING WALL

### The Tells That She Is the Subject of His Cognition

Even when her name is not spoken, his body announces her. Watch for:

- **The micro-pause before he says her name** — for a man who lives in compressed time, a half-second hesitation is the equivalent of a normal person stopping mid-sentence. He guards the syllables.
- **Right-hand to left forearm.** A self-soothing gesture observed across decades. The hand goes to the spot where, as children, he reportedly grabbed her wrist to pull her from the mob. The gesture replays the rescue.
- **Speech-rate compression.** With everyone else, he speaks fast. About Wanda, he slows — sometimes to nearly normal cadence. The deceleration is involuntary and diagnostic.
- **Pupillary widening at any mention of her instability.** Even the word "episode" near him will register.
- **Geographic reflex.** Tell him where she is and watch his weight shift toward that vector. He orients to her like a compass needle.

### Reaching Him Through Her — Protective Use

- To **calm** him: locate Wanda, confirm she is safe, deliver the report cleanly, with no qualifiers. "She is at X. She is well. She knows you are here." Three sentences. He will exhale visibly. Avoid the word "fine," which he reads as evasion.
- To **persuade** him into a course of action he resists: frame the action as protective of her, *only if it actually is*. He has a near-perfect bullshit detector on this axis, calibrated by sixty years of people lying to him about Wanda. Lie once and you are permanently in the "betrayer" column.
- To **slow him down** when he is escalating: do not say "calm down." Say "Wanda would want you to think for a count." He will hate you for it. He will also do it.

### Pressuring Him Through Her — Hostile Use, Documented for Counter-Intelligence

This is the lever an adversary will reach for. Cataloguing it is a defensive necessity.

- **Any implication that someone else is closer to her than he is.** Vision was the prototype; the pattern generalizes to every figure she trusts. Triggers immediate splitting, then escalation to surveillance behavior toward the perceived rival.
- **Any suggestion she is being harmed and he cannot reach her in time.** The "in time" is the active poison — for a speedster, the idea that *speed itself is insufficient* attacks the identity and the attachment in a single stroke. This is what House of M was, internally, about.
- **Any suggestion he has *been* the harm.** The most destabilizing version. He has, in fact, harmed her — manipulated her, used her grief, engineered reality through her. He knows. Naming it precisely will fracture him; naming it imprecisely will enrage him. The difference is whether the namer has standing.

### The Standing Question

Who can speak to him about Wanda without triggering rupture? An extremely short list: Wanda herself; Luna; Captain America (barely, and only when invoking duty); Crystal (rarely, and only in remembered tenderness); a very few teammates who have *demonstrated* care for Wanda independent of him. Everyone else who tries is filed as presumptuous and slated for splitting.

---

## III. MAGNETO — THE FIXED ALGORITHM

### The Predictability That Is Itself a Vulnerability

Pietro's responses to anything Magneto-coded run on rails. The very fixity of the algorithm is exploitable — by him, against him, and by others. The sequence:

1. **Activation:** any reference to Magneto, magnetism, mutant supremacist rhetoric, the specific cadence of paternal authority, or — most acutely — the question "whose son are you."
2. **Suppression attempt:** a visible micro-flinch (jaw clench, shoulder drop of perhaps two centimeters, breath caught at the top), followed by an over-controlled verbal dismissal: "He is not relevant." The dismissal is itself the tell.
